Major Fire in Hokkaido, Japan 97

250 houses burned down

Dentsu Telegram, Wakkanai, 1st - A fire broke out at the Minamikan Ryokan in Kitahama Street, Wakkanai Town, Hokkaido at 0:30 AM this morning. Due to the strong northwesterly wind, the fire quickly spread to the surrounding areas. The post office, government office, Hokkai Takushoku Bank branch, theater, and other major stores were all burned to the ground. The fire gradually subsided after 5:00 AM. Approximately 250 houses were burned down, resulting in huge losses. The prefectural authorities are currently seeking to provide relief.

116th Meeting of the Legislative Yuan 98

The Legislative Yuan held its 116th meeting at 9:00 AM on the 1st. Twenty-nine members attended, including Jiao Yitang and Shi Shangkuan. The meeting was presided over by Hu Hanmin. The following matters were discussed: (1) The Central Political Conference's 248th meeting's resolution on the draft principles for the examination and appointment of county magistrates was passed in accordance with the review opinions and sent to the Legislative Yuan for recording and reference. It was decided to send it to the Legislative Committee for review. (2) The Legislative Yuan's Labor Law Drafting Committee reported on the review and discussion of the proposal to extract excess profits from factories and stores in various places to subsidize the education expenses of workers' children and the construction expenses of workers' dormitories. It was decided to pass the review report, and it is not necessary to create separate regulations for this case. (3) The Legislative Yuan's Legislative Committee reported on the review of the draft Examination Review Regulations. It was decided that the Examination Review Regulations do not need to go through the legislative process, and the original proposal was returned to the Examination Yuan. (4) The Legislative Yuan's Finance Committee reported on drafting the National Government's Accounting Department Organization Law. It was decided to send it to the Finance Committee and member Jiao Yitang for reconsideration and review.

Uze’s Account of the Sino-Russian Conference 99

From our Shenyang correspondent: Uze, Director of the Library of the Chinese Eastern Railway in Shenyang, was summoned by Mo Teh-hui to go to Moscow on official business. After the opening of the Sino-Soviet Conference, he was again dispatched back to China to report on everything. He arrived in Shenyang on the 26th. Yesterday, this writer made a special visit to Uze's residence to record his account, as follows:

"The delegation to Russia arrived in Moscow on May 9th, and it has been more than half a year since then. Madam Mo, as well as Cai Gongzhi, Wang Yuebo, Wang Xinzhang, Nan Xianyi, Mr. Cui Shuyan, and the two ladies, Sun Suzhen, all live at No. 5 Little Kirov Street, the office of the Sino-Soviet Conference delegation. The four committee members, Liu Shaozhou, Li Yisun, Tu Dingfu, and Wang Nianjian, and the two secretaries, Wang Yunqing and Xie Zhongqing, all live in the Minde Hotel. The members of the delegation are extremely united in spirit abroad and all have a firm and enduring spirit to work hard for the country. In addition to their official duties, they also visit various places. Their handwritten diaries of their mission to Russia, one volume per month, contain detailed records and concise criticisms of the progress of the conference, the political situation and customs of the Soviet Union, and international trade relations. They plan to publish them as a book after returning home. Although Mr. and Mrs. Mo's diet and living arrangements are still comfortable, being far away in a foreign country, shouldering heavy responsibilities, and struggling in a difficult environment for half a year, one can imagine their hardship. On the 8th of this month, Mr. Mo met with Karakhan to discuss the date of the conference. Mr. Mo advocated for an early implementation, but Mr. Karakhan said that the Turkish Foreign Minister would arrive in Russia at the beginning of the month and would need to be received and seen off, so he wished to postpone it for a few days. Therefore, the two sides decided to officially open the conference on the 11th. The venue was chosen at the Foreign Ministry building, which is where the Soviet People's Committee for Foreign Affairs holds important meetings and receives foreign guests. The architecture is magnificent and the furnishings are rich and luxurious, resembling the Yingbin Hotel in Shidaren Hutong in our former capital. Those who accompanied Mr. Mo that day were the four committee members, Liu, Li, Tu, and Wang, the secretaries Cai Yunchen and Zhang Mingzhe, and the staff members Nan Wenming, Cui Shuyan, Ping Jie, etc. They all arrived at 5:00 PM. The Soviet Plenipotentiary Representative, Karakhan, greeted them at the door and shook hands with each of them. First, Karakhan and Mo talked briefly in a side room, and then they all gathered in the meeting hall. Karakhan gave a speech first and expressed his welcome. Then, Mo gave a speech. After the two sides spoke, they exchanged credentials. The procedures were all completed. Karakhan then asked the Plenipotentiary Representative of the Chinese government to clearly express his views on the Buriat-Mongolian Treaty Record. Mo advocated discussing issues such as the Eastern Railway in accordance with the powers conferred by the credentials. Karakhan still insisted on questioning about the Buriat-Mongolian Treaty Record. Mo, from beginning to end, based his arguments on the spirit of the government's February 8th declaration and argued with him. The debate lasted for three hours, and it was already after 8:00 PM. Because it was late, it was announced that the meeting was adjourned. This is the general situation of the official opening of the Sino-Soviet Conference. Although the meeting ended without a clear understanding, Mo's attitude can be said to be unyielding, indignant about the matter, and not disgracing the country. However, in the half year before the opening of the conference, Mo faced many twists and turns in negotiating the opening procedures. The first difficulty was on the Soviet side. Mo's credentials were specifically for discussing the aftermath of the Chinese Eastern Railway, while Karakhan's credentials were for discussing everything related to the Buriat-Mongolian Treaty Record, the Eastern Railway, trade, and the resumption of diplomatic relations. Karakhan believed that Mo's authority was insufficient and requested a change of credentials. Mo negotiated and protested repeatedly. After that, our Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent a telegram to the Soviet Foreign Ministry, stating that our Plenipotentiary Representative had the power to discuss the Eastern Railway, the resumption of transportation, and trade. However, Karakhan's attitude was still not satisfied. After repeated negotiations by Mo, Karakhan finally stopped nitpicking, which he himself considered a very large concession. This issue was delayed for a long time, and it seemed inconvenient to publish it at that time. These twists and turns from six months ago were also the reason why the domestic public opinion circles felt that the news was dull. Mo overcame this difficulty before the official conference could be held. Unexpectedly, it ended without a clear understanding due to the issue of the Buriat-Mongolian Treaty Record. How it will proceed in the future is still up to the two representatives to sincerely negotiate and depends on the sincerity of the Soviet Union towards the Sino-Soviet Conference. However, the newspapers in that country generally believe that the Buriat-Mongolian Treaty Record is a prerequisite for the conference. The commentary in their party's organ newspaper was full of criticism of our government, and the title was "Must Give a Clear Answer," which shows their attitude.

Regarding the recent reports in various newspapers that the delegation was preparing to return home, this is inaccurate. I have not heard Mo express this. As for Mo's trip to Leningrad, it was because after Mo arrived in the Russian capital, the Soviet Foreign Ministry, in addition to hosting visits in the Moscow area, also invited him to visit Leningrad (i.e., St. Petersburg) and the Caucasus and southern Russia, and to see the new constructions of their Five-Year Plan. Mo was unable to go before due to negotiating the opening of the conference. Now that the official conference has opened and the progress of the conference has been telegraphed to the government for instructions, he is taking advantage of this time to fulfill his appointment since Karakhan has also invited him to visit. When I left, I heard that Mo planned to leave on the 19th and return to Moscow on the 23rd. I left Moscow at 6:30 PM on the 16th. According to the itinerary, I should have arrived in Manchuria on the morning of the 23rd. However, because the dining car attached to the train derailed on the Ural Mountains at the border of Europe and Asia on the 17th, we were delayed for seven hours. Therefore, I arrived in Manchuria at 4:00 PM on the 23rd, Harbin at 1:00 PM on the 24th, and Shenyang on the 26th. During the seven-day journey, food was scarce, and bread and milk were often difficult to obtain, and there were often times when I had to endure hunger. Along the way, there were many new buildings and new agricultural tools that were still under construction, which were the beginnings of the Soviet Union's Five-Year Industrial Plan. When the train arrived at the Sino-Soviet border, it stopped for an hour. Special Soviet police inspected passports and checked luggage. All Soviet currency and works of art were not allowed to be taken out of their territory by passengers. The prohibition was very strict and the inspection procedures were also very complicated. However, Chinese delegation staff were treated very favorably when entering and leaving the territory. Therefore, I only had my passport checked and was not inspected. When the train left the Xiaozhan station, 66 li from the border, and entered Chinese territory, I felt a surge of joy in my heart. After another ten li to Manchuria, the train I was on was attached to the Chinese Eastern Railway Express. Looking out the window, the most heartbreaking thing was passing by the cemetery of the soldiers who died in battle last year in Zhalantun, which stood tall by the roadside." (October 28th)

Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi Begin Bandit Suppression 100

From our Hankou correspondent: Since He Chengjun returned to Hankou to preside over the war zone headquarters and convened a meeting with He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government, and Lu Dipin, Chairman of the Jiangxi Provincial Government, the voices of bandit suppression in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi have become very loud. The results of the consultations on the allocation of troops, the division of areas, and the funding arrangements have also been largely determined and implemented separately. The first to launch was Jiangxi Province. Most of the bandits, except for the two divisions of He Long and Kuang Duoxun on the border of Hunan and Hubei, and the Li Can division that occasionally harassed eastern Hubei, the remaining cadres such as Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, and Huang Gonglue all fled to Ji'an and Jishui in Jiangxi, which were successively captured. The authorities had no choice but to prioritize and start with Jiangxi Province. Recently, the troops supporting Jiangxi have been recruited by land and water. In addition to the original divisions of Zhang Hui Zan and Deng Ying, Hunan Province has sent the two divisions of Luo Lin and Li Jue to enter Jiangxi, and the Gong Bingfan division has entered Jiangxi from Hankou. Other divisions such as Tan Daoyuan, Mao Bingwen, Tai Shihui, Xu Kexiang, and the Peng Qibiao Brigade have also arrived one after another to encircle and suppress. The Wuhan war zone headquarters is still worried that the troop strength is insufficient and has specially transferred the two divisions of Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai to Jiangxi to assist. They are currently being concentrated separately to be transported by rotation. At this time, Hunan is in urgent need again. The bandits harassing Hunan suddenly captured Nanhua and have the momentum to counterattack Pingliu. He Jian has sent troops to suppress them on the one hand and telegraphed to the war zone headquarters to quickly allocate reinforcements on the other. He himself has also scheduled to leave for Pingliu within a few days to inspect. After receiving the telegram, the Hankou war zone headquarters, in addition to ordering the Qian Dajun division to temporarily stay in Hunan, will also add two divisions to enter Hunan from Hubei. There is also talk that a part of Xu Yuanquan's Forty-eighth Division will also be transferred to Hunan. He Chengjun has now issued an order that all troops designated to suppress bandits in the area must be deployed by the first day of next month and concentrated by the seventh day. The bandit suppression funds will be temporarily borrowed from the central government's new short-term treasury bills of one million yuan for application. It is reported that the bandit suppression military affairs in the Nanhua area have been quite smooth in recent days. If Wuhan sends a large army to assist, the Hunan bandits can be eliminated in one fell swoop. He Jian sent a telegram to Hankou yesterday to report on the bandit suppression situation as follows: "On the Nanhua side, the Sixteenth Division, Peng Weiren's division, has been ordered to suppress them. Sanxian Lake was recovered by Xiang Guangquan's regiment yesterday. The bandits retreated to Nanxian. The Sichuan Army Zhang's division arrived at Mahekou and has made contact with our army. Peng Dehuai's bandit division has returned to the area of Jietou and Sanyanqiao, attempting to attack Liu. Tao's division is suppressing them in Pingjiang. He Jian kowtows." (October 31st)

The Course of the Labor Dispute at the Dakang Cotton Mill in Qingdao 101

From our Qingdao correspondent: The Sifang Dakang Cotton Mill in Qingdao is run by the Japanese and employs about 4,000 male and female workers. Since August, labor-management disputes have occurred frequently. Recently, there has been a strike. The reason is that on the 11th of this month, a worker named Su Dingzhu was expelled by the factory for sleeping in the factory. The workers in the second workshop were greatly displeased and stopped working for three hours, and demanded that Su's job be restored within the day and that wages be paid during the shutdown period. The factory firmly refused to accept this, and the dispute was about to escalate. After consultation between the Bureau of Social Affairs and the Association for the Promotion of Civic Education, the factory was allowed to expel Su Dingzhu, and the remaining workers would not be held accountable. The wages for the shutdown period would be paid. Both parties have acknowledged this. At 10:00 PM on the 19th, the factory suddenly telegraphed the Bureau of Social Affairs, claiming that on that day, the workers in the fine yarn department of the first workshop had been engaging in slowdowns from day to night, and had been using wooden pipes to hit Japanese staff and Chinese foremen, obstructing them from performing their management duties, and requested that personnel be dispatched quickly to stop them. The Bureau of Social Affairs sent personnel to investigate. According to the workers, the reason why the workers were engaging in this behavior was that they were angry that the factory had reinstated Li Zhaohuan and Lü Xiben, the leaders of the Kedaohui organization. If Li and Lü were removed from the factory, it could be guaranteed that this would never happen again. The bureau immediately advised the factory to dismiss Li and Lü to avoid giving the workers an excuse, and sent clerk Deng Xin to proclaim this to the workers. On the 20th and 21st, the fine yarn departments of the first and second workshops of the factory had another slowdown due to the issue of shift changes. Then, Bureau of Social Affairs Director Yang Jinsheng personally engaged in practical negotiations with the factory's Tang Xian and the consultant of the Japanese Spinning Industry Association, Hiraoka Kotaro. After spending a long time, the factory finally managed to complete the shift change and restore work. On the 22nd, the workers in the fine yarn departments of the first and second workshops of the factory had another dispute over wages. The Bureau of Social Affairs negotiated with the factory again. As a result, the factory agreed to settle the wages for the 20th and 21st according to the average daily wage of the previous week. The workers were satisfied and resumed work as usual. In addition, the weft department of the weaving workshop also experienced slowdowns and demanded that the factory equalize wages. All of these were resolved through mediation by the Bureau of Social Affairs. At present, the labor dispute at the factory has been completely resolved, and the workers have all resumed work. However, the municipal government is still afraid that unscrupulous elements will disrupt the situation and specially issued a notice yesterday, advising the workers of the factory to work with peace of mind and not to be instigated by others, lest they incur blame and punishment. (October 29th)

Resumption of Direct Train Service on the Jinpu Railway 102

From our Jinan correspondent: Since the Jinpu Railway has been operating in sections, it has not only been inconvenient for merchants and travelers, but also the income of the railway has been greatly affected. It is reported that the Ministry of Railways has now negotiated with Zhang Xueliang, the Commander of the Northeast Border Defense, and reached an agreement to resume direct train service on the Jinpu Railway. From October 30th, the 90th passenger-freight mixed train operating indirectly between Jinan and Tianjin will be canceled. On the same day, the 1st and 2nd passenger trains will directly connect Tianjin. The 201st and 202nd Pingpu trains will also be scheduled to operate directly to Tianjin from November 1st, and then directly to Beiping after a short delay. The 1st and 2nd trains will operate daily, and the Pingpu trains will operate four times a week in each direction. The train schedule is as follows:

1st and 2nd Trains: The 1st train departs from Tianjin East Station at 8:20 AM daily, arrives in Jinan at 8:00 PM, and departs from Jinan at 8:30 PM, arriving in Pukou at 8:20 PM the next day. The 2nd train departs from Pukou at 10:00 AM daily, arrives in Jinan at 8:00 AM the next day, and departs from Jinan at 8:30 AM, arriving in Tianjin at 8:10 PM.

Pingpu Trains: The 201st train departs from Tianjin East Station at 9:25 PM every Tuesday, Thursday, Friday, and Sunday, arriving in Jinan at 9:00 AM the next day (i.e., Wednesday, Friday, Saturday, and Monday), and departs from Jinan at 9:30 AM, arriving in Pukou at 10:20 AM the next day (i.e., Thursday, Saturday, Sunday, and Tuesday). The 202nd train departs from Pukou at 6:30 PM every Monday, Wednesday, Thursday, and Saturday, arriving in Jinan at 7:00 PM the next day (i.e., Tuesday, Thursday, Friday, and Sunday), and departs from Jinan at 7:30 PM, arriving in Tianjin at 7:20 AM the next day (i.e., Wednesday, Friday, Saturday, and Monday).

Today (October 30th) is the first day of direct train service on the Jinpu Railway. After the 2nd train departed from Pukou, it was delayed for 9 hours and 3 minutes along the way, and finally arrived in Jinan at 5:20 PM. It departed for Tianjin at 6:10 PM. Gao Hengru, the Director of the Jinpu Railway Office in Jinan, has taken the train past Jinan to Tianjin to take over the Jinpu Railway Bureau and set up an office. (October 30th)

Guangzhou to Inspect Cinnamon Exports 103

Inspection will begin on November 1st

Exports will be permitted only after obtaining a license

From our Guangzhou correspondent: Since its establishment, the Guangzhou Commodity Inspection Bureau has required all export goods to be inspected before they can be declared for export. Previously, a disturbance occurred due to the inspection of wool. Now, it has been decided to implement the inspection of cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds for export from November 1st. When implementing the inspection, merchants should go to the bureau in advance to declare. Only after the bureau sends personnel to inspect and approve will a license be issued. Otherwise, exports will not be permitted. The inspection fee is one dime per dan (i.e., 100 catties). The detailed measures are as follows: (Article 1) These detailed rules are formulated in accordance with Articles 2 and 23 of the Provisional Regulations on Commodity Inspection. (Article 2) All cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds exported from Guangzhou shall comply with the provisions of these detailed rules and go to the bureau to fill out an inspection request form and submit it to the bureau along with the inspection fee for inspection. The request form mentioned above will be determined separately. (Article 3) Cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds that are bought and sold in the Guangzhou market and nearby areas may freely apply to the bureau for inspection if they wish. (Article 3) Cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds inspected in accordance with Article 3 may report to the bureau to verify the original packaging and exchange for an export certificate if they are transported for export during the validity period of the certificate. If the certificate expires or the packaging is not the original, Article 2 of these detailed rules shall still be followed. (Article 5) The inspection bureau shall dispatch personnel to take samples on the same day in the order in which the request forms are received. The sampling methods are as follows: (1) Four pieces shall be extracted for every 100 pieces or less, two pieces shall be extracted for every 50 pieces or less, and 8 taels (municipal system) shall be taken from each piece. (2) The extracted samples shall be mixed first, and the necessary amount for testing and the equal amount for re-inspection shall be extracted. The rest shall be returned. (3) The extracted samples shall be sealed and stamped by the sampler in the presence of the applicant to prohibit identification. (Article 6) The standards for qualified inspection are as follows: A. The ash content of cinnamon bark shall not exceed 5%, and the oil content shall not be less than 2%. B. The ash content of cinnamon tubes shall not exceed 1.4%, and the oil content shall not be less than 3%. C. The ash content of cinnamon seeds shall not exceed 3.4%, and the oil content shall not be less than 6.3%. The quality of the cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds mentioned above shall be clean and free of soil. (Article 7) Inspection procedures shall be completed within two days after sampling, and shall be extended accordingly on Sundays and other holidays. However, work may also be carried out as usual when necessary. (Article 8) Cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds that pass the inspection shall be handled in accordance with Article 13 of the Provisional Regulations on Inspection. However, the certificate to be issued shall notify the applicant to exchange for the certificate with the receipt given. The validity period of the certificate is three months, but it may be extended for two months if necessary. (Article 9) The bureau shall uniformly seal all qualified cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds on the packaging. (Article 10) The inspection fee for cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds shall be one dime per dan. Those who apply in accordance with Article 3 shall pay five cents per dan. However, when exchanging for an export certificate in accordance with Article 4, an inspection fee of five cents per dan shall be paid in addition. (Article 11) The original applicant may request a re-inspection once within ten days of receiving the notification after the cinnamon bark, cinnamon tubes, and cinnamon seeds have been inspected by the inspection bureau. (October 28th)

Therefore, the newspaper recorded the truth of the case in great detail. As for the Huang Xingan case (erroneously reported as Wang Xingan yesterday), who surrendered himself, he was the Deputy Director of the Field Tax Office during the tenure of Zhang Quan, the former Director of Finance. The Director was Cheng Lintu. Cheng fled after hearing the news after Pan Bin was arrested. Huang knew that he could not escape, so he came forward to surrender himself in order to be questioned. Since the beginning of the case, the provincial government has arrested Zheng Chengyuan, Pan Bin, Shen Zhiqing, Cao Qingzhi, Ren Shuchun, Di Zhen, Huang Xingan, and Zhou Shi in succession. Zhou Shi is currently the Director of the Fourth District of Liyang. Wang Rou, a member of the Third Division of the Provincial Government, secretly went to Liyang on the 30th to meet with You Bingzhao, the Director of the County Public Security Bureau, to draft a letter inviting Zhou to talk. Zhou came to the meeting without suspicion and was immediately arrested. The Public Security Bureau sent four police officers to escort him back to the province overnight with Wang. The reason for his arrest was that Shen Zhiqing had stated during interrogation that Zhou was friendly with Cheng Lintu. As a result, he was arrested. On the morning of the 31st, Qian Jiaxiang, the director of the Third Division, questioned him for a long time and continued to question Pan Bin and Shen Zhiqing. Ren Shuchun claimed that he was only a witness after being detained. Therefore, he was very uneasy and still treated people with the dignity of the Director of the Education Bureau, which affected the soldiers guarding him. He has now been ordered to close the door tightly and prohibit contact with outsiders. Di Zhen, the chief of the General Affairs Section of the Education Bureau, is still writing at his desk all day long, behaving as usual.

Changzhou 108

Funding for Dredging the Menghe River is Being Prepared: The Menghe River in Wu, Yixiang, Han River, has been shallow for a long time. Previously, a surtax on the land was levied to prepare for dredging. Dredging must not be delayed until this year. However, the estimated cost is about 180,000 yuan. Only 120,000 yuan has been collected. There is still a shortage of 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. The Menghe Committee has sent a letter to the Farmers Bank requesting a loan of 40,000 yuan using the land tax as collateral. Jiang Xichang, the director of the branch, reported to the head office supervisory committee for instructions to follow. The supervisory committee did not dare to approve it rashly and submitted it to the provincial government for submission to the 31st committee meeting for resolution. The resolution was approved, and the Dredging Committee has been actively proceeding.

Lawyers are Preparing to Form an Association: After the establishment of the Wuyi County Court, Zeng Chuxing, who is executing the initiation and organization of the association, has appointed three lawyers, Chen Yuansu, Lu Erchu, and Yun Kuiyao, to draft the articles of association. They have now been drafted and scheduled to meet today (2nd) at Chen Yuansu's law firm in Zhouxian Lane to discuss the matter.

Jiaxing 110

Escape Incident at the Third Prison: On the 1st, at approximately 1:00 AM, prisoners including Zhang Wuxian from cell number 11 of the Jiaxing Third Prison pre-dug a tunnel leading out of the prison gate. At the time, the north wind was howling fiercely. The prisoners took advantage of the strong wind to break out of the tunnel. Patrol officer Yin Zuo discovered the escape. When Yin discovered the prisoners had emerged from the tunnel, they held down his throat to prevent him from making noise. Patrol guard Wu Yunde assisted in the pursuit. Because Zhang Wuxian attempted to seize a firearm, he was shot and killed. Subsequently, three escaped prisoners were apprehended: Yu A-jin-fu (transferred from Pinghu, crime unclear), Zhang Songshan (convicted of theft in Wangdian, sentenced to seven years and six months), and Xie Yongming (convicted of trading opium, sentenced to three years and fined 120 yuan). On the afternoon of the 1st, at 3:00 PM, Shen Youqi, the local sub-court prosecutor, inspected the body of Zhang Wuxian (convicted of abduction, sentenced to one year imprisonment, already served four months), who was killed during the escape. He also instructed the guards to tighten security.

Water Police Apprehend Bandits: Xu Pucheng, the head of the Jiaxing Second Water Police District, recently learned that the Pinghu County area under his jurisdiction, as well as the Qingpu and Songjiang counties bordering Jiangsu Province, were frequently disturbed by gangs of criminals. He specifically ordered the patrol teams to proceed to the Pinghu and Liangyi areas for patrol. It is now reported that after the team arrived in Pinghu, they raided the Daying area of the county and arrested three bandits, Shi Sanhe, Shi Wen, Atai, and Tang Wenlong, who had robbed the Lin family. Eight sets of military uniforms and hats and one rifle were found at the home of Shi Azhang in Yang. The three bandits and the seized goods have been taken to Pinghu and are being held at the Ninth Team headquarters. They will be transferred to the district headquarters for interrogation in the coming days.

Haiyan County Steamer Detained: On the afternoon of the 30th, a fight broke out among river workers of the Haiyan Shen Zhi Company. County Magistrate Ruan received telegrams from the Public Security Bureau and immediately ordered the bureau chief to dispatch police and requisition the Xin Changan steamer from the Ningshao Company's Haiyan Xiashi route. By the time the crew and ship were notified, it was already 7:00 PM. Many crew members had already left. Finding personnel and starting the fire took time. The bureau chief also rushed to the scene. Due to the delay, the engineer was beaten. Wang A-lin was handed over to the security team for supervision. The county government also dispatched police to arrest the crew member Dezhen and sealed and impounded the steamer's engine room. As a result, the steamer did not operate on the 31st. It is now reported that the Jiaxing Ningshao Company believes that the steamer was subject to excessive requisitioning and abuse of power by the local government, infringing on freedom of property and obstructing traffic. It has telegraphed the provincial government to immediately release the steamer and investigate County Magistrate Ruan and the bureau chief.

Nantong 111

The Pinghu Banditry Case Becomes Increasingly Complicated: Zhang Kui, the district head of Pinghu, apprehended the bandits Wu Qin and Yang Jinyun and handed them over to the county government. After interrogation by the county court, they were found not guilty due to insufficient evidence and were released. Upon learning of this, the county government immediately dispatched police to arrest Wu and Yang and detain them, requesting instructions from the provincial government on how to proceed. District Head Zhang telegraphed to accuse Court Prosecutor Zhu. The families of Wu and Yang filed a petition with the court requesting relief. The court ruled that the Wu Qin and Yang Yun banditry case had already been dismissed and that if the county government arrested them within the scope of this case, it would be illegal. The matter should be investigated and a decision made. As for Zhang Kui's criminal behavior, the county government has been requested to remove him from his position and bring him back for questioning.

The Second County Administrative Conference Opens: The Second County Administrative Conference opened at the county government on the 1st. The opening ceremony was held at 1:00 PM. There are over 80 proposals, mostly concerning post-banditry recovery. The conference is scheduled to last for one period.

County Police Team Goes to Lüsi to Intercept Sea Bandits: Sea bandit Pan Kaiwu led more than 500 men to occupy Sanjia Town, and then gradually invaded the inland areas. Merchants and residents in the Tai Tuan area fled. The county police team has gone to Lüsi to intercept them.

Rugao 112

The Return of the Fengli Sea Bandits: The Fengli sea bandits had all left after being suppressed, but recently a large number of sea bandits have returned and become even more rampant. Along the coast from Shayuwa to Yangbei Port, there are more than 40 bandit ships, arbitrarily landing and extorting food and fresh water from the impoverished coastal residents. The residents are terrified. An elderly man named Sang Ruita, over sixty years old, was kidnapped by the sea bandits, who demanded 15,000 yuan. His family has already sent 10,000 yuan. The bandits recently sent a letter to his family with Sang's ear attached, dripping with blood, demanding 5,000 yuan within five days for his ransom, or else he would be dismembered.

Zhenjiang 113

Police School Graduates Go Missing Again: Graduates from the first class of the Police School, after being ordered to report to various counties to await assignments, often commit suicide due to not finding suitable work. Recently, it was reported that Dai Qichen, after being assigned to Taixian County, remained idle for three months. Subsequently, he was ordered by the department to transfer to Guanyun, but there has been no news for more than two months. A classmate from the Police School sent a letter to the Guanyun Public Security Bureau to inquire, but the letter was returned yesterday without anyone accepting it, and his family does not know his whereabouts. Whether he is alive or dead is unknown. It is unknown whether he suffered a misfortune. The police association is currently advertising for information.

Citizens Oppose the Construction of a Factory in a Prosperous Area: Merchants from Zhenjiang, including Shang Huo and Li Youlao, invested in building a four-story building in Xiaoying Houshen Ji Xiang to install machinery and open a flour mill. Merchants and residents of Yao Yiwan, upon hearing this news, believed that building a flour mill was related to a good enterprise and supported it. However, since it's close to where residents dwell, the residents believe that if the factory opens, the coal ash and smoke will pollute the air. Moreover, the noise from the machinery will disturb the residents' peace. They have jointly petitioned the provincial government not to approve it and to order the factory to find another open area to operate in.

Yangzhou 114

The Second Cavalry Regiment of the Instructor Division Comes to Yangzhou for Garrison: The Second Cavalry Regiment of the Instructor Division of the National Revolutionary Army is being transferred to Yangzhou in the coming days. Today (31st), the regiment specially sent Adjutant Wu Jimen to Yangzhou to contact the county government and public security bureau to arrange for garrison locations. However, there are many troops stationed in Yangzhou recently, and it is difficult to find temples. Moreover, cavalry requires pastures and must be stationed outside the city. It is reported that the Public Security Bureau is negotiating with Hongsi Temple outside the South Gate and Wutaishan outside the Bianyi Gate to serve as the regiment's garrison.

County Magistrate Investigates Embezzlement of Relief Funds: In Hongsi Temple in the western part of the county, there are more than 600 households of disaster victims. The Tenth District Office had previously submitted a register. When distributing relief tickets, over 600 tickets should have been distributed, but local disaster victims only received 249 tickets, a difference of 351 tickets. The households surrounded the local security guards and demanded answers. Currently, local citizens, including Wu Jin, have petitioned the county government to order the township head, Yu, to investigate and recover the funds to avoid embezzlement. After receiving the petition, the county government ordered the Tenth District Office to investigate and verify the matter.

The Airfield is Confirmed to be at Puqing Palace: The county government received an order to establish an airfield. It had previously jointly surveyed Puqing Palace in Dongguan and the Great Drill Ground outside the West Gate, submitting draft maps for review. Now, the Security Office has signed off on Puqing Palace, ordering the county to relocate the electricity poles and graves in the field according to the law and to build the airfield on the privately owned fields and houses in the field. Yesterday (30th), the county government issued a list of private farmland leased for use as an airfield at the Great Drill Ground for sixteen years to the Public Security Bureau for handling.

Huzhou 115

Five Bandits, Hong Cai Mao, etc., Executed Yesterday: The Second Regiment Headquarters of the city's Security Force extracted five key criminals from prison at around 3:00 PM yesterday: Hong Cai Mao (Henan), He Guang Fu (Hubei), Liang Jin Rong (Henan), Zuo Dong Qian (Henan), and Wang Wen Zhong (Shaoxing). They were verified, and escorted to the city's South Drill Ground for execution by firing squad. It is reported that all of them were guilty of kidnapping and murder.

Two Night Ships from Hu and Si Robbed by Bandits: At around 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 29th, two night ships, the Zeng Ji Heng Ji, left the city for Sian at the same time. While passing Hongxing Bridge, about three miles from Wushang Bridge, it was already late at night when they suddenly saw dozens of people on the pond road, each holding guns and flashlights, firing several shots and ordering the two ships to stop. The sailors on the two ships had no choice but to stop. The bandits then went to the two ships and searched the passengers one by one, with no one spared. Many of the goods on the ship were also robbed. It is reported that the two ships suffered heavy losses this time.

Pinghu 116

Zhoujiawei Town is Looted by Bandits: Zhoujiawei Town outside the east gate of the city was looted.

At around 9:00 PM the day before yesterday (30th), more than 30 bandits suddenly arrived, some wearing gray military uniforms, some wearing Zhongshan suits, all with wooden holstered pistols and speaking with northern accents. A bandit leader ordered his men to guard the east and west sides, fired a shot, and then began looting in different directions. First, they robbed Wang Tongmao's Yichang butcher shop, then the Dongxi Zhang Xinchang rice shop and Wang Xiechang's grocery store, losing about 200 yuan. Ding Qiaxing's dried goods store and Zhang Yongsheng lost about 400 yuan. The Xinchang Feng Yang cloth shop was completely looted. The Shunxing Store Jiang Tongshun, Xitongmao dyeing shop, and others lost a total of three or four thousand yuan. The shop owner of Zhang Yongchang, Guangming, was severely tortured and his injuries were serious. It is estimated that the entire town lost more than 10,000 yuan. The looting lasted for two hours. The sound of police whistles was constant. The bandits then fled to the southeast. The town has reported the incident to the county for investigation and apprehension.

On October 15, they went from Xinchang to Tangtian, occupying the village for two days and nights. United forces of Youzhuping, Tangxi, Luchu, Longtan, Lijianfan, and Pingken six village security corps initiated an attack and fierce battle for two hours capturing two bandits. The bandit's troops gradually withdrew and then looted and set fires in nearby villages such as Hutang, Huixi, Dongjiaan, Yujiakeng, Cheng Dakeng and Tingxia causing much damage. The six village security corps, felt weak and telegraphed the governments of each county for assistance. Also, they worked hard to defend. It is now known that the bandits have escaped into the Dalai area of Siming Mountain.

Bengbu

Bandit Atmosphere on the Border of Henan and Anhui: The border area between Henan and Anhui has been ravaged by bandits for many years, and the people have suffered greatly. In previous years, Li Laomo and Li Kebang led more than 10,000 people to disturb the territory of Fuyang, causing great local losses. Since Li Laomo was executed and Li Kebang was pacified, the bandit atmosphere has slightly subsided. Although there are scattered bandits, the whole county of Fuyang has organized people's self-defense corps, with considerable self-defense capabilities, so a small number of bandits dare not do harm. Unexpectedly, in late this month, more than 1,000 Henan bandits sneaked into the northwest territory of Fuyang, breaking villages and forts in succession, with a very rampant momentum. The bandit suppression headquarters in Anhui Province recently received a quick telegram from Zhao Rui, the magistrate of Fuyang County, and immediately ordered the 135th Regiment of the 45th Division under its command, as well as Liu Zixin, the commander of the 270th Regiment stationed in Fuyang, to quickly lead his troops to suppress the bandits. After receiving the order, Commander Liu is now assembling his troops and cooperating with the people's self-defense corps to advance and suppress the bandits.

Telegrams to Teachers and Students to Prepare for Closing

Zhang Naiyan, President of Central University, telegraphed yesterday to the heads and directors of various departments, stating that the Nanjing Central University Documents Section should forward to the secretary and the heads of all departments: "I am determined in my intention to resign. I hope that you all will prepare to close and hand over matters as soon as the new president arrives." I am determined in my intention to resign and will not return to school. Please, deans and teachers, take separate responsibility for maintaining order to avoid disruption. I am deeply hopeful." Naiyan Eastern telegraphed to the students, stating that the Nanjing Central University Student Union should forward to all students: "I am very grateful. However, I am determined in my intention to resign and do not wish to return to school. I hope that you will all focus on your studies, study diligently, and quietly await the government's solution. I hope for this." Naiyan Eastern.

Unrest in Jiangsu Education 122

Differences of Opinion Between the Director of Education and Provincial Schools

There has been a state of unrest in Jiangsu education recently, stemming from Chen Hexian's tenure as Director of Education, during which he has been extremely isolated from Jiangsu education and unwilling to accept any input from the education sector. He consistently ignores appeals, and the arrears in educational funding are increasing daily. Teachers and staff cannot maintain their livelihoods. Representatives have been rejected when seeking audiences to discuss the matter, leading to accumulated resentment and brewing turmoil. It is said that some school principals are stepping forward to mediate, advising the authorities to change their attitude in order to cooperate, fearing that the loss of Jiangsu's educational spirit after the outbreak of turmoil would be difficult to recover. It is also heard that the central government is paying close attention to this matter, and there is talk of an exchange of education directors between two provinces, which may not be unfounded.

Beijing Municipal Education Bureau Revises Draft Bylaws on Pension for Vocational Educators 125

The pension regulations for school vocational educators were originally promulgated by the central government's Ministry of Education, but the length of service required and the amount of the pension were too high, making implementation difficult. The Beijing Municipal Education Bureau, noting that some vocational educators in the city have died after continuous service of three or five years, but were unable to receive pensions due to legal restrictions, has found their dedication to public service and their posthumous circumstances deeply regrettable. Director of Education Zhang has drafted a simplified version of the pension for vocational educators in Nanjing Municipal Schools, requesting the Ministry of Education to slightly amend the length of service requirement. Director-General Jiang of the Ministry of Education received him and praised the proposal, agreeing to adopt it as much as possible when revising the regulations. At the same time, the bureau has submitted the draft bylaws to the municipal government for approval and filing. The draft bylaws are excerpted below:

Simplified Bylaws on Pension for Vocational Educators in Nanjing Municipal Schools: 1. The pensions for vocational educators in municipal schools in this city shall be handled in accordance with these bylaws, in addition to complying with central government regulations. 2. Vocational educators in municipal schools in this city who meet one of the following conditions may receive a pension: (1) Death after continuous service of three years or more (2) Death after continuous service of five years or more. 3. The pension payment standards are as follows: Full-time vocational educators who meet the first item of Article 2 shall receive two months of their final monthly salary; those who meet the second item shall receive three months of their final monthly salary. 4. The calculation of years of service shall be limited to continuous service in one school, except when the transfer to another school is with the permission of the school chief, or approved for special reason by the school head. 5. To claim a pension, each school must have its legal heirs submit a fact-filled application and the claimed amount, which shall be submitted by the school chief to this bureau, and the bureau will dispatch personnel to investigate and verify it before submitting it to the municipal government for approval and allocation. 6. These regulations shall be implemented after being discussed and decided by the bureau's affairs meeting and submitted to the municipal government for approval.

Guangdong Provincial Education Conference Concludes 126

Summary of Resolutions Made in One Week

The situation of the Guangdong Provincial Education Administration and Secondary Education Conference during its first day of meetings has already been reported. The conference was held for seven consecutive days. The articles of the proposals of each group are lengthy and cannot be recorded in detail. Here is a special summary of the key points of the resolutions made by each group each day during the week: The 21st was the second day of the conference. 96 members attended the Education Administration Group, and 153 representatives attended the Secondary Education Group. The proposals were reviewed in groups as follows: (A) Education Administration Group: The first group, with 21 members, discussed local education administration agencies. The second group, with 14 members, discussed and reviewed education funding. The third group, with 10 members, discussed and reviewed compulsory education. The fourth group, with 8 members, discussed and reviewed primary education. The fifth group, with 7 members, discussed and reviewed social education. The sixth group, with 5 members, discussed and reviewed women's education. The seventh group, with 8 members, discussed and reviewed investigation and statistics. The eighth group, with 8 members, discussed and reviewed school establishment standards. The ninth group, with 11 members, discussed and reviewed supplementary education. (B) Secondary Education Group: The first group, with 24 members, discussed and reviewed the school system and curriculum. The second group, with 18 members, discussed teachers and staff. The third group, with 12 members, discussed and reviewed management. The fourth group, with 12 members, discussed and reviewed school buildings. The fifth group, with 69 members, discussed and reviewed equipment. The sixth group, with 18 members, discussed and reviewed funding. On this day, the meeting was held from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM, and from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM. Each member reviewed the proposals in groups in order, and the results showed that they were generally appropriate, with occasional supplementary reasons or methods. The 22nd was the third day of the conference. 95 members of the Education Administration Group attended and resolved (1) "Local Education Administration Agency Proposal" (2) "Local Education Funding Proposal". 133 members of the Secondary Education Group attended and resolved "Secondary Education Program". The 23rd was the fourth day of the conference. 81 members of the Education Administration Group attended and continued to discuss "Local Education Administration Agency Proposal" and "Local Education Funding Proposal". 228 members of the Secondary Education Group attended and resolved "School Responsibility Proposal". The 24th was the fifth day of the conference. 81 members of the Education Administration Group attended and continued to discuss the "Local Education Funding Proposal" and passed the "Compulsory Education Proposal". 129 members of the Secondary Education Group attended and resolved (1) "Teacher and Staff Responsibilities and Job Assignments Proposal" (2) "Teacher and Staff Treatment and Security Proposal" (3) "Teacher and Staff Training Proposal" (4) "Management Training Proposal" (5) "School Health Proposal" (6) "School Sports Proposal" (7) "Teaching Proposal" (8) "Performance Assessment Proposal". The 25th was the sixth day of the conference. 84 members of the Education Administration Group attended and resolved (1) "Primary Education Proposal" (2) "Women's Education Proposal". 103 members of the Secondary Education Group attended and continued to discuss the "Performance Assessment Proposal", passed it, and resolved "Forms and Records Proposal" and "School Buildings and Equipment Proposal". The 26th was the seventh day of the conference, which was also the last day. 77 members of the Education Administration Group attended and resolved (1) "Investigation and Statistics Proposal" (2) "School Establishment Standards Proposal" (3) "Social Education Proposal" (4) "Adult Supplementary Education Proposal". 108 members of the Secondary Education Group attended and resolved "School Funding Proposal". At 11:00 AM that morning, the proposals of each group were resolved, and the closing ceremony was immediately announced. Representatives from the Administrative Education and Secondary Education Groups gathered in the auditorium to perform the ceremony as usual. Chairman Jin Zengcheng delivered a speech, stating that the most difficult thing for Guangdong education now is education funding. Due to the military expenses since the military uprising, the education funding cannot be paid. Secondly, the change in the cowhide tax rate by the Finance Department also affects education funding. As for education administration itself, the heads of education bureaus in various counties often fail to handle the official documents of the Education Department in a timely manner, and they also fail to report the amount of education funding that each bureau should increase, which hinders the preparation of the education funding budget by the Education Department. He hoped that everyone would pay attention to this point in the future. It was past 1:00 PM, and the meeting was adjourned (October 26).

Zhejiang Education Department Improves Kindergarten Education 127

Planning to Establish a Kindergarten Normal School

Researching Improvement Methods

The Zhejiang Education Department believes that if the foundation of kindergarten education lacks perfect facilities, it will greatly affect the future of education. It has found that this province has not paid attention to kindergarten education, and the existing kindergartens lack qualified teachers. Therefore, it has decided to plan the establishment of a provincial kindergarten normal school within this year, and at the same time research the various facilities of the existing kindergartens and methods of improvement, stipulate the standards for establishing kindergartens, and urge various counties and cities to establish kindergartens and daycare centers to promote and advocate it.

City School Administration and Training Discussion Meeting 128

Held Yesterday at the City Education Bureau

Since the beginning of this semester, the City Education Bureau has convened subject-specific discussion meetings for teachers and staff of various city schools in Chinese, arithmetic, and nature. Yesterday, it convened another administration and training discussion meeting. More than 30 schools attended, with over 70 principals and directors of training from various schools. The meeting commenced at 1:45 PM, with Supervisor Ma Chonggan presiding. After reports from administrative and training inspectors, discussions began on all proposals. Administrative section: (1) For the sake of neatness, should children have uniforms, but can exceptions be made for children from families with economic difficulties? (Lu Bin) (2) If the school's administrative organization is too strict, it will be too cumbersome in handling affairs; if it is too simple, it will be perfunctory. How should this be remedied? (3) If affiliated primary school affairs are concurrently managed by the middle school, there will be delays in handling matters. How should this be remedied? (4) How should girls' interest in daily public service be aroused? (Above, Wuben Affiliated Primary School) (5) Issues concerning standards for complete primary schools. (6) Should primary schools have the power to expel students? (Above, Xicheng) (7) Is it necessary to hold city school administration discussion meetings once a month? Since President Hu took office, the school's affairs have been steadily improving. We are planning grand strategies for future development. If a change of personnel occurs midway, it will inevitably require starting anew, which is greatly detrimental to the school's progress. Consider that in European and Western countries, principals hold long-term positions; this is the principle. Furthermore, a university is the highest educational institution in a country, the source of specialized talent nationwide, and the focus of domestic and international attention. Someone without adequate qualifications and prestige cannot be entrusted with leading the school. The so-called qualified and prestigious individual must have a considerable position in the national academic community in terms of personal scholarship and morality to be able to lead the academic community and be qualified to lead a university without being a mere figurehead. This is one reason. A university president cannot be compared to a university professor. Even if scholarship and morality are adequate, experience in handling affairs is still necessary. Someone without maturity, stability, an age of over forty, and significant achievements in previously managing higher education cannot shoulder this important responsibility. This is another reason. Furthermore, Tongji University primarily focuses on medical and engineering schools and has a long history. Someone who cannot deeply understand the situation, thoroughly perceive the environment, and is proficient in German cannot cope adequately and achieve success. This is the third reason. The above only mentions the most important points. After careful consideration, the students believe that there is no suitable candidate other than President Hu in the country. The students are deeply concerned about the school's future and dare to sincerely express their concerns. We hope that the Ministry will listen to our heartfelt plea and earnestly retain President Hu to reassure the community. We are immensely anxious and await your response. Furthermore, rumors are circulating that a certain Mr. [omitted] will become the president, causing panic and consternation throughout the school. We believe that the Ministry, for the sake of the school's future, would not make such a decision. In haste and urgency, we await your instructions.

Four University Volleyball Tournament Soochow Wins Championship 137

Two to One Victory Over Jinling

The result of the first day of the Four Universities Volleyball Championship was that Zhejiang University violated the rules and Shanghai University forfeited, and the situation gradually stabilized. Jinling itself also had the confidence to win the championship. The knowledge that what it planted was not what it harvested has made the championship go to Soochow with a ratio of two to one and won its fourth championship. Soochow has won its third consecutive championship, which seems to be lucky this time, but its strength is enough to be seen in East China. The process is as follows:

First Game Won By Jinling

Yesterday the weather was cloudy, but fortunately there was no rain. The audience was fascinated by the ball game. The more interesting it became, the more people gathered on the Tiangci Zhuang Road in the afternoon. It can be seen that ordinary people pay quite attention to one or two wins and losses. The game started at two and a half o'clock. The referee, Mr. Li Feiyun, blew the horn to summon the generals. Soochow served first. Zhu Zhilun's long shot was immediately returned by Jinling. Fortunately, the split down was weak and rescued into the enemy's camp to open the record. Zhu Sheng launched a fierce attack and won two more goals in a row. Then Jinling had a serving opportunity and delivered it back and forth. Team leader Yu Huanzi ambushed to save the dangerous situation and stretched his arms to suppress the battle, showing great magic and creating a 5-5 situation. Soochow's cheerleaders rose up to cheer. Jinling's lineup was very neat and well-organized. Tan Tianli stood alone, invincible. After coming and going, there was no easy game. From five to six to five to nine, Soochow attacked. When it was Zhao Congheng's turn to serve, the ball was like a pressure from the sky, which shocked Jinling. Jinling scored six consecutive points and reversed the situation to 11-9. After changing positions, Jinling's attack was still strong, and the momentum suddenly turned around, and they continued to score points and took the lead again. Finally, at the critical moment of life and death, they were tied at twenty to twenty and Jinling escaped the first game. Jinling won the first game with a score of 22 to 20, but it was also dangerous.

Second Game Won By Soochow

At the beginning of the second game, Jinling did not dare to underestimate Soochow, who had deep roots, and was very careful. After the opening ball, Soochow missed a shot and scored two consecutive points. At this time, Zhao Congheng from Soochow rose up and won four consecutive points. Zhou Zhaogang and Mei Jiaxiang worked hard to attack and also won four goals. In the first half, Soochow's situation was dominant with eleven to. After changing positions, Soochow scored eight points, while Jinling had no way to twist the split and only scored six points. As a result, Soochow won 21 to 12.

Third Game Won By Soochow

After the second game, the victory or defeat was not decided, so the game continued. In the third game, Jinling was very flat at the beginning. Soochow scored five consecutive points, the lineup was greatly disrupted, and the morale was scattered. They were in a slump. In the first half, Soochow took the lead with eleven to four. After changing positions, Soochow no longer worked hard, but the momentum had already been created, and Jinling could not recover. Yu Huanzi only called out in vain and only saw Soochow's rapid rise. As a result, Soochow won the championship with a score of 21 to 9 with a ratio of two to one.

Members of the Two Teams

Soochow Team First Row Zhu Zhilun Zhou Zhaogang Zhao Congyan Second Row Mei Jiaxiang Zhao Rupin Qiu Zhuoping Third Row Xia Chuzhang Zhou Peilin Lv Gaohui

Jinling Team First Row Huang Zhongqing Huang Bin Hong Liu Zhong Third Row Tan Tianli Yu Huanzi Li Ruizhen Third Row Feng Meilin Pan Jieming Wang Dejin

Shanghai University Statement On Terminating The Match 138

The Shanghai University Athletic Guidance, Ni Xiaotong, specially sent a letter yesterday to clarify the facts regarding the termination of the match between Jinling and Shanghai University in the East China Four University Volleyball Championship. The original letter is transcribed below:

Dear Sir/Madam, Today I read in your column on November 1st that there was "Shanghai University expressed opposition before the start of the second game and the game was not finished" in the East China Four University Volleyball Championship. This is not in line with the facts and I would like to request a correction. According to the East China Four University Sports Association Charter, if there is rain during a ball game, it may be postponed if both parties agree. If one party does not agree, the game must continue. When our school was playing volleyball against Jinling, it was already raining heavily. After the first game ended, the referee directly negotiated with the Jinling athletic guidance and players to stop the game. Afterwards, the referee and Jinling players left the court. Our school believed that since the first game had ended in the rain, the second game should naturally continue. Otherwise, before the start of the first game, the referee could have solicited the opinions of both parties to determine the proceedings. In addition, the referee did not solicit our school's opinion before leaving the seat, which was not the attitude that a referee should have. Our school tried hard to argue with him and wanted to continue the game, but the referee still insisted on stopping the game. Therefore, our school could not tolerate this violation of the charter and decided to withdraw from the game. As for the report that Jinling wanted to continue and Shanghai University objected, it is too far from the truth. The facts are all there and cannot be fabricated. Please correct it immediately for the sake of virtue. Sincerely, Ni Xiaotong, Shanghai University Athletic Guidance, November 1st

Special Issue No. 2 of Shen Bao National Industry and Commerce Conference

First Day of the Industry and Commerce Conference 147

Opening Ceremony Held in Beijing Yesterday Morning at Ten O'Clock

First General Meeting Continued to Review in the Afternoon

Review Meetings of Each Group Will Be Held This Morning and Afternoon

The Industry and Commerce Conference, which has been prepared for three months and is attracting national attention, opened in Beijing yesterday. Members paid respects to the mausoleum at 8 AM and the opening ceremony was held at the Zhizhi Society at 10 AM. The first general meeting was held in the afternoon, and the groups reviewed in the afternoon. The groups will review this morning and afternoon. Here is a record of yesterday's events.

My Views on Foreign Commerce and Domestic Commerce (Zheng Hongnian) 148

The commerce that the state recognizes and should develop in cooperation with the people broadly includes two types: one is domestic commerce, and the other is foreign commerce. Domestic commerce has the same ethnic customs, laws, taxes, credit affairs, educational system, and so on. When the national politics are good and various production industries are developed, domestic commerce tends to promote those areas with better production and coerce those with inferior production to improve. Both tend towards areas with superior living conditions, so the national, social, and people's livelihoods, finance, material culture, and functions are not only not harmed by this development, but can also be promoted to a higher level. However, foreign commerce, in areas different from one's own country, is different.

Since the advent of world international trade, the livelihood policy of foreign commerce has occupied a special position. The powers of the East and West have almost used the power of the whole country to support their foreign policies because their domestic population has increased, industry has developed, and production has been excessive, making it impossible to match the ordinary progress of the people's livelihood. They have had to find other markets abroad or, due to a lack of raw materials, have had to rely on other countries and transport industrial products in exchange in order to meet the national balance of income and expenditure and seek a surplus in their budget. Therefore, foreign commerce should not be observed as a business of buying and selling goods, but only by observing how the facts of foreign goods entering and domestic goods leaving affect the entire domestic people's livelihood production. The state's foreign trade has claims, such as exports of goods whose value exceeds the value of imports, which is called export exceeding, also known as the balance of payment surplus. The state's foreign commerce has an import value greater than exports, which is called import exceeding, also known as the balance of payment deficit. The more a country wants to retain and increase its common wealth domestically, the more it should attach importance to foreign commerce, comparing the import and export of goods. If there is a deficit in the balance, money flows out and wealth decreases, it is considered a great danger to the national economy and people's livelihood. For this reason, the importance of foreign commerce is more obvious than that of domestic commerce. Colbert's argument that the interests of foreign commerce are national interests is still supported by political scholars and they are unwilling to abandon it. According to customs reports, China's imports of foreign goods are increasing year by year. The impact of the increase in foreign goods has greatly changed the historical allocation of labor and capital used in domestic production industries, resulting in domestic production and business being increasingly suppressed. Except for the introduction and transportation agency of foreign goods, there is no commerce to speak of. If we want to solve the problem of revitalizing national commerce, the livelihood policy of foreign commerce is very different from the policy that should be implemented for domestic commerce. In the latter, the most important issue is the cooperation between labor and capital in industry and commerce, and price adjustment is the design of producers and consumers, such as whether the organizational form of commerce and the dependency relationship of the national livelihood should be concentrated in large stores and exchanges, whether consumer cooperative enterprises should be favored, and whether the safety of the current situation of small merchants should be taken into account. Should fixed commerce and itinerant commerce be treated differently? What is the most appropriate form of commercial enterprise and trading method? If the direction and implementation policies are determined, the state will not have to worry. However, foreign commerce changes with the international environment. First, we must understand the quantity and types of imports from foreign countries and exports from our own country, and then establish precise plans to regulate foreign trade. On the one hand, we must promote domestic production to the greatest extent, and on the other hand, we must reduce the competitive power of foreign goods against domestic goods. In particular, we must pay attention to industrial products, using tariff protection policies, subsidies, or prohibiting the export of domestic raw materials to make foreign goods expensive and domestic goods cheap. In addition, domestic transportation should be improved to ensure that the transportation of commercial goods is fast and efficient. This will increase domestic production and ensure that industry and commerce have good production conditions. In addition to these measures, if domestic production is considered to be related to the people's livelihood, a complete system that does not support or promote it, or uses national financial resources to promote domestic industry and prevent foreign competition, then the impact of foreign commerce on domestic commerce will be great. Even if it cannot quickly reach a superior international position, the balance of payments can be maintained.

Hopes for the Conference (Li Quanshi) 149

This time, the National Government's Ministry of Industry and Commerce convened the Industrial and Commercial Conference to vigorously implement industrial and commercial policies, promote the development of production, foreign trade, and increase the national economy. It is indeed a microcosm of a national economic conference, because except for agriculture, industry, mining, fisheries, transportation, and other matters not within the scope of discussion, the rest, such as matters concerning the relief of national unemployment, matters concerning industrial relief, matters concerning international trade, matters concerning industrial, commercial, and financial matters, matters concerning the concentration of capital and the use of foreign capital to develop industry, matters concerning labor welfare and labor-capital disputes, matters concerning scientific management, matters concerning commercial taxes, matters concerning industrial raw materials, matters concerning the promotion and protection of domestic goods, matters concerning the improvement of state-owned products, and matters concerning basic industries, etc., are all included in the major matters that are closely related to the national economy.

Since the scope of discussion planned for the Industrial and Commercial Conference is so broad, the importance of its responsibility can be imagined.

It is heard that the ministry has already received more than two hundred proposals, so the urgency and complexity of its affairs can be imagined. I, as a member of the experts, hope that all the members attending the meeting will select one or two groups according to their own expertise, carefully review the proposals belonging to each group, spread public opinion, and formulate complete and meticulous plans for submission to the general assembly for a public decision. The general assembly should especially avoid making speeches that fill the hall without much conclusion.

Furthermore, after the general assembly of members has made public decisions on various proposals, the power to implement them rests with the government. However, we hope that after the government has gathered ideas and formulated plans, it should not only hear the sound but not see the facts. As the saying goes, governing is not about talking too much. We only hope that the industrial and commercial authorities can muster a spirit of fearlessness to relieve the people from their suffering.

Paying Respects at the Mausoleum 150

At 8:00 a.m., all the members, led by Kong Xiangxi and Zheng Hongnian, went to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum to pay their respects. The members who attended included Huang Puqi, He Chongjie, Zhang Xinwu, Shao Jinqing, Miao Chengshi, Wu Yun Chu, Li Houshen, Zhang Shude, Zhang [Blank], Xu Dongfan, Ye Huijun, Wu Daye, Cai Shengbai, Zhou Qibang, Wu Jingqing, Pan Xulun, Zhang Zilian, Xu Yongzuo, Chen Yizhou, Ren Sida, Rong Zongjing, Zhang Enzhang, Li Deyong, Pan Gongzhan, Hu Shuhua, Zheng Shouz芝, Lao Jingxiu, Tang Jisan, Lu Chengzhang, Wang Yuansong, Deng Yanhua, Liu Mianz執, Chen Anren, Wang Jiean, Li Yishi, Zhu Funan, Zhao Jinqing, Shou Jingwei, Lu Guangji, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Huiyuan, Lü Xizhai, Ma Zezhao, Wang Yiting, Zhu Maocheng, Zhang Yujing, Shi Youming, Yu Shushen, Qian Fenghao, Zhong Weicheng, Liu Wanqing, Zou Bingwen, Huang Shoumin, Wang Yiting, Chen Zheqing, Li Kuian, Wang Binyan, Chen Riping, etc. In advance, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce made a copper wreath with the words "Respectfully Dedicated to the Right of the General Manager's Spirit and the Industrial and Commercial Conference" inscribed on it, which was displayed in front of the stone statue of the General Manager in the sacrificial hall. Grand Opening Ceremony 152

(1) Consolidate Industry, Commerce, and Finance (2) Collaborate on Industrial Construction
