(5) Revitalize Inherent National Products (6) Develop Foreign Trade

丨Pay Attention to Psychological Construction

One, Preserve Inherent Virtues

Two, Absorb New Commercial Knowledge

Today, the National Industrial and Commercial Conference opens, and construction authorities from all provinces, industrial and commercial leaders, labor mentors, and economic experts gather together to sincerely discuss matters and accept the participation of personnel from various central party and government agencies. Xiangxi bows to it.

More Than Eighty Public Organizations in Shanghai Request the Conference to Reconsider the Issue of Trade Regulations 155

Yesterday's Telegram Urged Wang Yansong and Others to Strive for It

Shanghai Intestine Industry, Egg Industry, Shoe Industry, Cotton Fluffing Industry, Fruit and Local Goods Industry, Domestic Pigment Miscellaneous Goods Industry, Sauce and Wine Industry, Cosmetics Industry, Western-Style Wooden Furniture Industry, Cured Meat Industry, Transportation Industry, Miscellaneous Retail Industry, Chinese Woolen Fabric Factory Industry, Spring Chair Industry, Pawnshop Industry, Chinese Soap Industry, Material Bottle Industry, Wood Industry Explosives Industry, Steel and Tin Industry, Chinese Candle Industry, Silk and Satin Industry, Duck Slaughtering Industry, Pollen Industry, Tea Food Industry, Hotel Industry, Candle Industry, Ice Factory Industry, Shoe Leather Nail Industry, Western Pigment Industry, Brass Woodworking Industry, Pen Measurement Industry, North-South Goods Demolition Industry, Liang Shaoxing Wine Industry, Noodle Industry, Tooth Bone Ware Industry, Timber Industry, Straw Hat Industry, North Goods Industry, Longan Industry, Hat Shop Industry, Fresh Meat Industry, Rickshaw Industry, Paper Industry, Sand Boat Number Industry, Oil Hemp Industry, Chinese Medicine Industry, Flying Flower Industry, New Medicine Industry, Gauze Number Industry, Chicken and Duck Industry, [Blank] Industry, Fresh Pig Industry, Restaurant Industry, Staple Binding Industry, Comb [Blank] Industry, Bamboo Industry, Advertising Industry, Medicinal Material Industry, Western-Style Flower Board Chair Industry, Seafood Grocery Industry, South Goods Industry, Postal Transportation Industry, Rice Number Industry, Clothing Industry, Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry, Paint Industry, Ham Industry, Brick Ash Industry, Sugar Industry, Color Printing Industry, Sauce Garden Industry, Ginseng Bird's Nest Industry, Tobacco Exchange Industry, Parasol Industry, etc., more than eighty trade associations, because the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Standing Committee Member Wang Yansong has always been concerned about the situation of various industries, and Wang is also a member hired for this National Industrial and Commercial Conference opened in Beijing. Yesterday, Wang was specially telegraphed to strive for the issue of trade regulations. The text said: "To Wang Yansong, member of the National Industrial and Commercial Conference Secretariat in Nanjing: I have learned that since the Shanghai Municipal Business Transport was led by you, all the past complicated organizations have been reorganized into trade associations in accordance with laws and regulations. The great achievement of unification is truly a grand event for all ages. Every time I think about it, I am deeply respectful. The responsibility of the trade association, according to the laws and regulations, is to maintain and promote the common interests of the industry and to correct the malpractices of the business. However, the promotion of public welfare must have its methods of promotion, and the correction of malpractices must have its tools of correction. What are these methods and tools? They are the trade regulations formulated by the trade associations with reference to the habits of the industry. However, these formulated trade regulations must be observed by all members inside and outside the association in order to take effect. Otherwise, not only will the trade association be unable to fulfill its declared responsibilities, but also China's commerce will never have any hope of improvement. Therefore, since the newspaper reported that 'the Ministry of Industry and Commerce discussed and rejected the resolution of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Members' Congress that the trade regulations submitted by the trade associations for approval should be regarded as special regulations formulated by the official authorities for the industry, and all industries that have not joined the association should also abide by them,' everyone has been terrified, telling each other and appealing to reconsider. In Shanghai, I have been honored to have been seen twice by Mr. and have agreed to provide assistance with great enthusiasm and deep admiration. Now that the National Industrial and Commercial Conference has opened and Mr. is invited to attend, I urge you to hold firmly, submit the reconsideration, and also ask Yu Hede, Xu Jiyin, Wang Xiaolai, Ye Huijun, and Fang Jiaobo to strive together to achieve the goal. I think that the discussing officials are all outstanding talents of the time. For the issue of trade regulations that is equally important to the unified commercial operation, they will certainly maintain the original intention of Fu Que businessmen and people."

Sheng Shenjue deeply believes that whether the industrial and commercial undertakings of our country can grow and prosper from this and open up a new beginning will be determined by the results of this conference. In addition to happiness, I really cannot express my infinite prayer.

The establishment of the foundation of industrial and commercial enterprises in any country in the world and the degree of its continued growth are all determined by the industrial and commercial policies decided by the government, and the industrial and commercial policies adopted by any government are determined by whether the domestic industrial and commercial groups can cooperate with the government to determine their success or failure. Therefore, at the beginning of the establishment of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Xiangxi first proposed the two meanings of official-civilian cooperation and labor-capital coordination as the standard for future political implementation, because the government and the people are one, and their pain and prosperity are closely related. If the government is the government and the people are the people, not only will industry and commerce not be improved, but also the future of the country will not be able to achieve stability.

Xiangxi has the talent but heavy responsibility, and at times is worried about accidents. However, today is the difficult time for the country's creation, and the responsibility for the protection and promotion of industry and commerce lies in the responsibility. Therefore, following the General Manager's Principle of People's Livelihood, based on the party's program, examining the current social situation and industrial and commercial conditions, the outline of industrial and commercial administration and the work plan during the training period have been determined and implemented in sequence. Among the important ones are: (1) Soliciting industrial and commercial opinions and arbitrarily formulating industrial and commercial laws and regulations in order to adapt to the social situation; (2) Consulting with the competent authorities to consider the current industrial and commercial situation and jointly revise tariffs to protect fledgling industries; (3) Establishing the Central Industrial Inspection Institute and the Bureau of Weights and Measures to gradually realize the standardization of industry and commerce; (4) Establishing the Commodity Inspection Bureau and the Industrial and Commercial Visiting Bureau to improve the quality of domestic goods and pay attention to foreign publicity in order to increase the credit of foreign trade; (5) Establishing the China National Products Exhibition and organizing the China National Products Bank to cultivate the people's habit of loving and using domestic goods and to support the development of domestic goods production institutions. All of these are actively carried out within the limits of talent and economic capacity, but they have not made long-term progress due to environmental limitations. Regarding the international aspect, in order to seek international cooperation, exchange industrial and commercial knowledge, and promote domestic industrial and commercial progress, representatives have been selected to attend the International Chamber of Commerce, the International Raw Silk Conference, and the International Labor Conference. Recently, it has been proposed to the National Government to establish a currency standard to relieve the panic of expensive gold and cheap silver, and to abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes to seek the reform of the commercial tax system and improve the transportation organization in order to eliminate the obstacles to industrial and commercial development. However, industrial and commercial construction is complicated and requires gathering ideas and wisdom. I hope that the scholars will come forward. The previous two committees of the Ministry, the Industrial and Commercial Design and the Industrial and Commercial Laws and Regulations, have already received the assistance of industrial leaders, economic scholars, and legal experts, and have made many plans. This time, the military is over and peace is seen again, and the National Industrial and Commercial Conference that Xiangxi expected in his inaugural declaration is also held at this time. It is the first time that the central government of the National Government has made up its mind to support our industrial and commercial circles, and it is also a plan to get rid of the old and establish the new, cooperate with the people to establish a century-old plan, and seek the prosperity of the national economic construction. It is also the beginning of the active cooperation between the government and the industrial and commercial circles. The beginning of the power of the people. I would like to mention a few points for discussion: One is to consolidate industry, commerce, and finance. The reasons for the insufficient development of industry, commerce, and finance in our country are indeed very complicated. The lack of funds, the high interest rate, the lack of investment protection, and the chaotic currency system in various provinces are indescribable. The excessive rise and fall of the exchange rate of gold and silver are also among the most important. From now on, how should we establish a currency standard, consolidate industry, commerce, and finance, and how should we protect the rights and interests of Chinese and foreign investment, and retreat from the general speculative frenzy, will be the responsibility of those who are concerned about industrial and financial affairs to carefully consider and properly plan for the future. The responsibility lies with the industrial and commercial community, and I hope that they will carefully discuss it. This is the cure for the disease. The second is to collaborate on industrial construction. Industry is more important than commerce in safeguarding the national economy and the people's livelihood. The basic industries that our country urgently needs at present, the Ministry has prepared a plan and presented it to the National Government to give priority to the establishment of fine yarn, woolen weaving, triacid, and sugar factories to show promotion. I hope that we can work together to see its success as soon as possible. The third is to improve industrial and commercial organizations. Commercial groups in our country have gradually been reorganized, and labor groups have also been reorganized in accordance with the law. However, the reorganization is not in its name but in its essence. The future direction should be to follow the party's program to refresh the spirit and organization, and to refer to the practices of Europe and the United States to pay attention to investigation and research so that industrialists and businessmen can gradually develop according to their basis. At present, the labor-capital dispute, which is regarded by all sectors of society as a major reef in industrial development, can also be easily and appropriately resolved scientifically, benefiting both parties. The fourth is to promote scientific management. In the past, commercial types in our country were all sticking to conventions and standing still, while industry was still in its infancy and formed its own atmosphere. The violation of scientific principles in its management methods cannot be overstated. In May of this year, Xiangxi and his colleagues initiated the organization of the China Industrial and Commercial Management Association to promote scientific management, improve production efficiency, and realize the Principle of People's Livelihood as the only goal. Although the scale has been established, the promotion of interests cannot be achieved overnight. The fifth day is to revitalize

Photo of Members Visiting the Mausoleum Yesterday Morning (Taken by Nanjing Guanghua) 156

The Grand Opening Ceremony Yesterday (Taken by Nanjing Guanghua) 157

Inherent national products. Our country is rich in natural resources, and inherent specialties are also numerous. However, either the production volume is too small to meet the needs of society, or the quality is uneven and cannot meet foreign standards. It should be rectified and remedied by promoting mergers and operations and carrying out large-scale production as the fundamental plan. The sixth day is to develop foreign trade. Our country has seen more and more people surpass us in the past twenty years, and the silk, tea, tung oil, soybean, and other special products that occupy the most important position in export trade have been stifled by the fierce competition from foreign countries, and there is a great tendency to move forward and retreat and to grow and diminish. As a result, clothing, food, housing, and transportation are almost all dependent on foreigners, and the economic difficulties are frightening. In order to save the situation, the fundamental plan is to persuade the implementation of protective tariffs and reward export policies. However, the organization of the International Trade Commission and the National Export Trade Association is also an urgent task. I hope that we will strive to fight and turn defeat into victory.

As for what the commercial community in our country should pay more attention to in psychological construction, there are two points: One is to preserve the inherent virtues and establish industrial and commercial integrity. The old customs of our country have always valued integrity, and once a word is spoken, it will not change for a long time. The credit of Chinese merchants is recognized by foreigners, that is, the beautiful relationship is also due to the fact that other countries value profits. The late General Manager deeply regretted that the restoration of inherent virtues was emphasized, and the meaning was precisely here. On the second day, we should absorb new industrial and commercial knowledge and strive for international friendship. In this era of scientific omnipotence, the industrial and commercial progress of European and American countries is almost a thousand miles a day. The backwardness of industry in our country is undeniable. From now on, we should allow the absorption of new knowledge and strive to improve. Only we must not be self-satisfied and deeply closed and refuse. We still hope to go further and encourage the industrialists and businessmen of various countries to grind each other.

The above is just a brief outline of Xiangxi's feelings. The participants are all experts and hold the same vision. I hope that on the one hand, they will express their knowledge and experience and contribute as much as possible to the construction plan of the industrial and commercial undertakings of our country for the government to adopt. On the other hand, they will examine the needs of various industries and contact them to carry out the work in order to overcome the current difficulties and strive for the actual cooperation between the government and businessmen and between businessmen and businessmen. The industrial and commercial undertakings are deeply dependent on it, and the bright future of the party and the country will also be determined by the success of this conference.

Chairman Jiang's Instructions 158

丨Develop Industry and Commerce丨Utilize Foreign Capital丨

Today, the National Industrial and Commercial Conference opens, and it is the time when the military affairs have ended and the unification has been completed. The chief officials in charge of industrial and commercial administration in various provinces and cities and economic experts from all over the country, as well as industrial and commercial leaders from home and abroad, have gathered together with a spirit of hard work to create a precedent for cooperation between officials and civilians. It is an unprecedented event in the industrial and commercial community. In addition to being happy, Zhongzheng cannot help but say a word to punish you.

Our party has inherited the General Manager's instructions, investigated the national situation, and issued declarations at the past national congresses and the Central Executive Committee, all of which have focused on protecting industry and commerce, developing the economy, and promoting the people's livelihood as the goal. This should be seen and heard by all the participants. Our country is vast and rich in resources, and its workers are hardworking and thrifty. Commerce has always valued integrity and is recognized by the world. However, the remnant warlords have repeatedly rebelled, and the bandits and communists in various places have taken the opportunity to make troubles, which has led to many misfortunes in the country and hindered the progress of construction. Now that the rebellion has been successfully suppressed and order has been gradually established, it is appropriate to gather the strength of the whole country to seek the progress of industry and commerce to benefit the people's livelihood, and the foundation of the country depends on the government and the people working together to strive for rapid progress. From the perspective of responsibility, it is the responsibility of the government to eliminate obstacles with negative policies and to promote and encourage with positive policies. However, the development of industry and commerce cannot be achieved solely by the government's strength, and its foundation lies in the industrial and commercial community itself. How to improve products, how to refine technology, how to promote sales, how to maintain inherent integrity, and how to develop natural resources are the issues that the industrial and commercial community must strive to do. How to strengthen the group, how to coordinate labor and capital, how to circulate finance, how to compete in foreign trade, and how to adapt domestic supply and demand are the issues that the industrial and commercial community must strive to help each other. If, in view of the fact that our country's science is young and capital is lacking, how should we import foreign capital for use under the principle of equality and mutual benefit in order to increase production and extend the use of foreign experts to take charge of technology? This is also what the General Manager has shown in his instructions and what we can follow. As for the participants, all of you are the backbone of the industrial and commercial community and have the responsibility to assist the government in implementing industrial and commercial policies. You also have the position of guiding and supervising the general public. I hope that you will express your opinions, discuss them in detail, determine the plan, and look forward to implementing it together to establish the foundation of the economy and bring the people's livelihood to prosperity, then the holding of this conference will not be in vain.

Sun Ke, Representative of the Central Party Headquarters 159

丨Support the Kuomintang丨Engage in Economic Construction

Sun Ke's address briefly stated that he was very honored that the Industrial and Commercial Conference was opened today and that experts from all over the country were gathered together. However, in addition to being happy, he also had a few feelings. Now that the country is unified and the military affairs have ended, we should strive to engage in construction. The most important point of the proposal is to develop the economy. Only when the national economy develops can the country develop and make progress. The industrial and commercial community throughout the country should work together to support the government's plan. All the difficult problems encountered by the government and the industrial and commercial community in economic construction are hoped to be resolved in this conference. If specific measures are discussed, they can be implemented. General Jiang Kai's victory once generated a feeling about party affairs, but since the Northern Expedition of the party from Guangdong, reactionary warlords have always tried to resist. Therefore, the party affairs have not been reorganized and have not been completely satisfactory. This is inevitable, but the party's two enemies are the warlords and the communists. If we do not support the Kuomintang, we will either go to the warlords or the communists. This is how dangerous it is. Therefore, seeking national stability and economic development can only be achieved by supporting the Kuomintang to lead the country and supporting the Kuomintang to build. It is even more important not to hate the Kuomintang. Behind the communists is the Third International. Russia, during the imperial system, always thought of invading China. Now it is propagating communism, which is still a disguised method of invasion. The Chinese people should not be fooled by it. The points mentioned by Minister Kong Fang are all the key points for today's economic construction and the development of industry and commerce. I hope that all the participants will have detailed research and achieve extremely satisfactory results. I wish the Industrial and Commercial Conference will pass all the resolutions and see them implemented in the future, and I wish you all good health.

Speech by National Government Representative Wang Chonghui 160

丨Emphasis on Industry and Commerce丨Not Just Lip Service丨

I am very honored to represent the National Government at this grand gathering. There are many reasons for the underdevelopment of industry and commerce in China. Besides material reasons, spiritual reasons are particularly important. Historically, China has placed industry and commerce after scholars and farmers. Examination methods were used to encourage scholars, and prayers were used to develop agriculture. However, industry and commerce were looked down upon, and this concept has been around for a long time, resulting in the current backward situation of industry and commerce. The so-called "industry" and "commerce" of the past are not the same as today's. Since the invention of machinery in the last hundred years, industry and commerce have been very different from the past. Because in the past we emphasized industry and commerce, reactionary elements could destroy it at any time. Today's emphasis on industry and commerce is not just lip service, but also to reform the long-standing habits of industry and commerce and to eliminate the obstacles to the development of industry and commerce. Premier Sun Yat-sen, in his busy schedule, drafted an industrial plan to promote the development of industry and commerce. The Premier said in this plan that if the power to develop industry and commerce is not developed automatically, and if the power of development is in the hands of others, then China will perish. Therefore, the existence of the power to develop industry is very important to the survival of the country. The goal of this conference is about four things: (1) to promote industrial and commercial policies; (2) to develop foreign trade; (3) to develop commercial enterprises; (4) to promote national economic power. Today, the members present are either commercial leaders or experts and representatives from various provinces and cities. In the future, they will definitely work hard to realize a new era of industry and commerce in accordance with the purpose of the conference, creating a new era of cooperation between the national industrial and commercial circles and the government.

First General Meeting 161

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - The first general meeting was held in the afternoon, and chairmen were elected for six groups.

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - The meeting divided into six groups, each electing a chairman. The first group is Zhang Xinwu, the second group is Ren Sida, the third group is Ma Chaojun, the fourth group is Lin Kanghou, the fifth group is Hu Shuhua, and the sixth group is Pan Gongzhan.

Grouping of Proposals 162

Divided into six groups for review

Two hundred and seventy-seven proposals

In accordance with the rules, the various proposals are divided into six groups, and a table of contents is compiled and printed for members to check.

The first group of proposals concerns industrial and commercial policies and administrative regulations, totaling sixty-two proposals.

The second group of proposals concerns international trade and transportation, totaling thirty proposals.

The third group of proposals concerns labor welfare, labor disputes, and scientific management, totaling twenty-seven proposals.

The fourth group of proposals concerns industrial and commercial finance and taxation, totaling sixty-three proposals.

The fifth group of proposals concerns the development of industry and the promotion, protection, and improvement of domestic products, totaling seventy proposals.

The sixth group of proposals concerns national unemployment and industrial and commercial relief, as well as other matters, totaling twenty-five proposals, for a total of two hundred and seventy-seven proposals.

Group Review 163

First Meeting of the First Group

丨Sixty-two Industrial and Commercial Proposals丨

丨Divided into Five Subgroups for Discussion丨

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - The first review meeting of the first group was held at 3:00 PM. Chairman Zhang Xinwu had Wei Tingsheng read out the sixty-two proposals of the group one by one. After the reasons for the proposals were explained, it was decided to divide them into five subgroups for discussion according to the type and nature of the proposals: (1) Industrial and Commercial Protection; (2) Industrial and Commercial Organization; (3) Industrial and Commercial Research and Improvement; (4) Industrial and Commercial Laws and Regulations; (5) Industrial and Commercial Training. The second review meeting will be held on the morning of the 2nd.

First Meeting of the Second Group 164

International Trade Divided into Four Groups for Discussion, Full Review on the 2nd

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - The second group review meeting was presided over by Ren Sida. The thirty proposals submitted to the conference for review were divided into four subgroups: 1. International Trade Organization; 2. The relationship between transportation, security, and industry and commerce; 3. Special Products; 4. Commodity Inspection Regulations and Standardization of Export Goods. Each committee member identified with one subgroup, and it was decided that the subgroups would meet separately at the Central Hotel at 8:00 AM on the 2nd, and a full review meeting would be held at the Zhizhi Society at 2:00 PM to report on the results of the subgroup reviews.

First Meeting of the Third Group 165

丨Labor Issues Divided into Seven Categories for Discussion丨

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - Ma Chaojun, Lu Bohong, Shou Yicheng, Zhu Maozheng, and others attended the third group review meeting. Chairman Ma appointed Yan Zhuang and Huang Zupei as documentation committee members. As a result of the review, the twenty-seven proposals submitted to the conference for review were divided into seven categories: (1) Labor Law; (2) Scientific Management; (3) Labor Movement Guidelines; (4) Labor Education; (5) Labor-Management Cooperation; (6) Labor Welfare; (7) Labor Unemployment Relief. The committee members will identify with one or two types and hold meetings on the 2nd to review them. A report will be submitted to the conference on the 3rd.

First Meeting of the Fourth Group 166

Divided into Financial and Commercial Tax Reviews

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - Twenty-five people attended the fourth group review meeting, which was chaired by Lin Kanghou. As a result of the review, it was decided to divide the sixty-three proposals submitted to the conference for review into two categories: (1) Finance, with thirteen people appointed to review; (2) Commercial Tax, with twelve people appointed to review. Wu Yunzhai, Hu Ziji, Qian Xinzhi, Zhang Gangbo, and Yuan Duanfu were appointed as organizing committee members. The organizing committee will begin work on the morning of the 2nd, and a joint review meeting of the Financial and Land Tax categories will be held starting at 2:00 PM in the afternoon.

First Meeting of the Fifth Group 167

丨Review of Seventy Proposals丨

丨Six Review Standards Determined丨

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - The fifth group review meeting was held at 4:00 PM, with thirty-six review committee members attending. Hu Shuhua chaired the meeting. The group's proposals totaled more than seventy. It was decided that the review standards would be the following six items: (1) Basic Industry; (2) Indigenous Industry; (3) Promotion of Domestic Goods; (4) Industrial Raw Materials; (5) Industrial Standards; (6) Others. The cases will be incorporated into various departments according to their respective natures so that they can be discussed at the meeting tomorrow morning.

First Meeting of the Sixth Group 168

丨Two Proposals Approved and Sent to the Conference, Two Proposals Reserved, One Proposal丨

丨Relief for Various Industries and the Unemployed丨

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - At the sixth group review meeting, chaired by Pan Gongzhan, the first proposal to request the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to inform industrial and commercial sectors nationwide to gather and study their own pain points in order to find ways to provide relief; the fourth proposal to instruct chambers of commerce in various locations to inform various industries and gangs of their operating difficulties or successes, and to request that the government assist or provide relief in detail, to be discussed at each meeting of the chamber of commerce to promote commercial development, were both approved. The second proposal to promote handicrafts to relieve various unemployed and vagrants, and the third proposal to suggest ways to relieve the failure of Cantonese silk foreign trade, were both sent to the conference for discussion. The fourth proposal to suggest allocating funds to deposit in public and private banks in Guangdong and Zhejiang provinces to maintain the balance of silk cocoon values was decided to be reserved.

Review Today 169

Six Groups Held Separately in the Morning and Afternoon

Nanjing, 1st Telegram - The conference issued a notice on the evening of the 1st that review meetings will be held in the morning and afternoon of the 2nd, in the following order: First group at 8:00 AM, second group in subgroups in the morning and full review at 2:00 PM in the afternoon, third group at 8:00 AM, fourth group in subgroups in the morning and full review at 2:00 PM in the afternoon, fifth group at 8:00 AM, sixth group at 8:00 AM. Except for the second group, which will meet in subgroups at the Central Hotel in the morning, the rest will be held at the Zhizhi Society.

Researching the National Calendar for Closing Accounts 172

The Chamber of Commerce Approved the Process of Staggered Methods

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has Specially Formed a Specialized Committee to Review

Proposing to Take the Day Before Lichun as the Final Closing Date

Closing accounts according to the national calendar is a matter of great concern to the society. Its relationship is not only in the business community, but also with the general public. The reporter of the New Voice Society stated that the staggered method of closing accounts according to the national calendar was originally decided by the Shanghai Special Municipal Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee and then presented to the government for approval and implementation. This year, the industries felt the difficulty of its implementation, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has also accepted the research and formed a special committee to review it. Therefore, this reporter specially visited Mr. Yan E, the secretary of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, to explain in detail the process of this case as follows:

The original letter of review regarding the national calendar for closing accounts: According to the national calendar for closing accounts, the Shanghai Special Municipal Social Bureau sent a letter to the Shanghai Special Municipal Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee for review on September 9th of last year. The original letter stated: "From next year (i.e., the 19th year) onwards, the annual staggered collection of accounts should be in accordance with the calculation of the solar calendar, or according to the solar terms, the year before and after should be appropriately divided into several periods, and it must be for the purpose of abolishing the lunar calendar. Please inform your association to check and refer to the above methods, examine the commercial situation, participate in opinions, and formulate this year's (18th year) unified closing date and the staggered method of collecting accounts from next year onwards, so as to prepare for adoption and shelving the case in anticipation of speedy implementation." According to the original letter from the Social Bureau, there are two methods: one is staggered periods and the other is according to the solar terms. Its sole purpose is to abolish the lunar calendar and abide by the national calendar.

The situation of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee's review: After receiving the above letter from the Social Bureau, the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee first conducted a detailed study by the Standing Committee, and then submitted it to the eighth plenary meeting on September 30 for discussion. It was decided that the promotion of the national calendar and the abolition of the lunar calendar should be unanimously observed in accordance with the government's order. However, the closing of accounts by lunar calendar in the business community was originally divided into three periods a year, and the end of the year was the major closing. If the number of closing periods is increased, the period will be short and the implementation will be difficult. If the number of periods is reduced, the economic circulation will be difficult. In order to facilitate the facts of all parties, it is still appropriate to close accounts in three periods a year. As for the staggered method, our country is based on agriculture, and we must take into account the harvest season of farmers. It is found that the end of May in the national calendar is the time for silkworms and barley to appear, and September is the time for rice to ripen. If the end of May and the end of September of the national calendar are used as the closing dates for the business community, there will be little obstacle in the implementation. It is still appropriate to use the end of December of the national calendar as the major closing date, etc. After the discussion, the three committee members, Wang Yansong, Bei Songsun, and Qin Runqing, were first recommended to contact the Social Bureau, and it was deemed feasible before the official letter was replied to the Social Bureau on October 4.

Various opinions during the review: When the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee reviewed this case, although some members of the consolidation committee advocated setting another commercial calendar, the majority of the committee members believed that since there was a determination to implement the national calendar, there should be no concerns first. If it is resolutely decided and it is indeed difficult to pass in fact during the first session, the government can also clearly understand that it is not that merchants are complacent and unwilling to reform, or perhaps other flexible methods can be set. At that time, the Nanjing Municipal Social Bureau also sent a letter to solicit the opinion of the Nanjing General Chamber of Commerce on the method of closing accounts according to the national calendar from the 19th year onwards. After discussion, the Beijing Chamber of Commerce believed that the three periods of May, August, and the end of the year of the national calendar were satisfactory as the closing periods and sent a letter to the Beijing Municipal Social Bureau for submission to the Beijing Municipal Government for submission to the National Government for record. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee decided on this three-period method because the opinions of the Beijing and Shanghai Chambers of Commerce were consistent on the national calendar's year-end closing period.

The process of the National Government's approval and notification: After receiving the letter from the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee, the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau submitted it to the Municipal Government. The Municipal Government believed that the proposed reform of the closing date method was still detailed and asked the Executive Yuan for instructions. The Executive Yuan also ordered the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to review and reply. Afterwards, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce replied that it was in line with the central laws and commercial customs and that the proposed method could be approved so that the national closing date could be unified and the old calendar could be fundamentally resolved. It was replied to the Executive Yuan. The Executive Yuan re-examined and found no differences and submitted it to the National Government for review and filing. In addition to asking the National Government to issue a notice to the whole country to comply with it, the Shanghai Municipal Government was ordered to forward the notice to the Social Bureau and reply to the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee. The letter stated: "However, from the 19th year onwards, the staggered method proposed must be strictly followed for closing accounts." At the same time, the Municipal Party Department and the Special Zone Provisional Court forwarded the notice to the association, and the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee distributed letters to all trade associations and published announcements in newspapers to inform them. Afterwards, if local chambers of commerce sent letters to inquire, the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee would immediately record the letters and reply to them.

The promotion of the national calendar for closing accounts this year: Since the official establishment of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, it has been working hard to implement the national calendar for closing accounts. Before the end of May and the end of September for closing accounts, it will first publish announcements in newspapers to enable merchants in the city to comply at the time. The Money Industry Association, the Coal Industry Association, the Silk Industry Association, and other associations also published announcements in newspapers to remind their members to pay attention and comply. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce also closed its office for one day at the end of May and September to draw the attention of merchants. After the end of September, the Money Industry Association published announcements in newspapers stating that the national calendar year-end closing was approaching, hoping that all industries would prepare in advance. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce also decided at the fourth executive committee meeting to publish announcements in various newspapers in the city and send letters to all trade associations in the city to prepare for the national calendar year-end closing to show its determination to comply with the national calendar. Each party stated the situation of hardship: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce first received a letter from the Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce on a certain day of a certain month stating that there might be difficulties in the national calendar year-end closing this year and requesting the government to specially approve a flexible extension of one and a half months to solicit consent. After receiving the letter, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of the Standing Committee to discuss that the extension of one month last year due to insufficient preparation was originally a temporary transitional measure. This year is the second year of implementing the national calendar, and merchants have long heard about it, and it seems inappropriate to change the method of closing accounts at the end of May, the end of September, and the end of December, etc. However, at that time, the Qianye Association of six counties in Jiangsu Province, including Jiangning, Suzhou, Wuxi, Wujin, Danyang, and Zhenjiang, sent representatives to Wuxi to hold a meeting. Because of the difficulty in implementing the year-end closing of accounts, they decided to request the establishment of a commercial and civil accounting year, with the end of January of the national calendar as the major closing date. At the same time, representatives of chambers of commerce in various counties in Jiangsu also held a meeting in Zhenjiang and unanimously approved the proposal of the Qianye Association of six counties to request the establishment of a commercial and civil accounting year, and added the opinion that the deadline for collecting grain silver in each county should be extended from the end of December to the complete end of February 15 of the national calendar so as to take care of the facts and avoid difficulties. The Qianye Association of six counties and the representatives of the chambers of commerce of 39 counties jointly submitted a report to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for filing. At the same time, the soybean and rice industry, fresh pork industry, pollen industry, ginseng and bird's nest industry, fruit and local goods industry, hat industry, transfer and customs declaration industry, new medicine industry, and silk and satin industry in this city all stated the various difficulties in the practical situation of closing accounts at the end of the year in accordance with the national calendar, hoping that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce would collect the opinions of various industries and submit them to the government for modification.

The Chamber of Commerce Specially Forms a Review Committee: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, based on the fact that various parties have requested and realized that the commercial situation really needs to be reconsidered, submitted the entire case to the fifth executive committee for detailed study. The committee members present on that day included Ye Huijun, Luo Qinghua, Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, Fang Jiaobo, Zhu Wenqi, Lu Fengzhu, Lu Wenshao, Xu Jiyi, Zhu Yinjiang, Wu Zhonghao, Shen Lanting, Lu Qisheng, Lao Jingxiu, and other 14 people, who all expressed detailed opinions on this case. After discussion, it was believed that this case was of great importance to commerce and that a special committee should be formed to collect opinions from all parties to study and properly handle it. Zhu Yinjiang, Lu Wenshao, Luo Qinghua, Wang Yansong, and Xu Jiyi were immediately appointed as members of the special committee. The special committee convened a meeting at 2:00 PM on October 30. After review and research, it was believed that since closing accounts in accordance with the national calendar was the only principle that had already been decided, there could be no changes, but there should be room for requesting modification as to which day of the national calendar could actually be implemented in the business community. It was found that our country is based on agriculture and the national economy is related to agricultural harvests. The Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee decided to use the end of May, the end of September, and the end of December as the closing periods, but there were two shortcomings: (1) The end of May and the end of September both took into account agricultural harvests in the original letter from the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee to the Social Bureau, but the end of December's major closing period did not pay attention; (2) If the end of December is used as the final closing period, then the closing dates for the second closing date will be five months from January 1 to the end of May, the second will be four months from June 1 to the end of September, and the third will be only three months from October 1 to the end of December. This 5, 4, 3 method is too uneven. Although the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee had this method at the time, its purpose was to resolutely promote the national calendar and it had its own special intentions. However, now that there are difficulties that cannot be solved in fact, it is of course necessary to seek remedies. In order to remedy this difficulty in fact, it is proposed to refer to the letter from the former Social Bureau to the Chamber of Commerce Group Consolidation Committee and modify the method of dividing the periods according to the solar terms, with the day before Lichun as the final closing period for the business community every year. The reasons are: (1) The Lichun climate is calculated according to the solar calendar and there is no suspicion of using the lunar calendar; (2) Lichun is always on February 4th of the national calendar every year, and even if there are changes, it will be on February 5th, with a difference of only one day, and the dates can be calculated and determined; (3) Before Lichun, the agricultural harvests have long been completed and the income of farmers has been converted into cash. There are no problems with collecting accounts and paying payments in cities and towns; (4) If February 4 is set as the final closing period, then the three closing periods can make up for the too short third period with the too long first period, which is more even. It is heard that the committee members researched repeatedly and all believed that it was appropriate, and it was decided to report to the Executive Committee for discussion and approval before submitting it to the government for filing.

More than one million yuan has been collected since the collection began

Landlords in the Chinese area request to stop collecting

Special Tax Cargo Ship Runs Aground on the Upper Yangtze and is Robbed 184

Entire Ship of Special Goods Looted

Losses Reach Hundreds of Thousands of Gold

Now Being Transported by China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Ships

The Special Tax Bureau in Lianghu has a special bureau for open transportation. Each month, there are two shipments from Sichuan to Wuhan for public collection

Page 14

The special tax is levied under the guise of prohibition and prevents the malpractices of smuggling by unscrupulous merchants. It is reported that recently, the ship carrying this cargo suddenly had an accident en route, and all the goods were stolen, resulting in losses of hundreds of thousands of gold. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has now dispatched ships to transport the goods. The details of this incident are as follows:

Amount of Special Goods Transported to Wuhan: Since the establishment of the Special Tax Bureau, the amount of special goods from Sichuan imported into Lianghu has been limited. The director of the bureau, Li Muqing, agreed with the cargo owners in Sichuan to set a monthly limit of 1,000 tons, divided into two shipments, each carrying 500 tons, which means a total of 16,800 dan per month. Within this limit, the bureau issues stickers with the seal of the Lianghu Special Tax Bureau to indicate publicly taxed goods. Goods without this special stamp are subject to detention and heavy fines. The ship carrying the goods is also dispatched by the bureau to ensure caution, and an armed guard platoon is assigned to the ship to provide security.

Cargo Ship Runs Aground: The ship dispatched by the Special Tax Bureau to transport the goods, called the "Shudu", has a capacity of only 500 tons. On this occasion, it was fully loaded with special goods in Yichang. When it reached a place called Tiaocheng, the water level in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River was shallow. The ship's draft was heavy, and it ran aground on a shoal in the river due to careless navigation. The ship was stuck in the sand and mud, unable to move. Unexpectedly, after running aground, a robbery occurred.

Special Tax Goods Stolen: This year, there have been more bandits on the upper Yangtze River than in previous years. The road is not peaceful. Communist bandits and other bandits are everywhere, specializing in robbing merchant ships. After the "Shudu" ran aground, it was about to report to Wuhan for help, but the bandits learned that there were not many guards on board. They gathered a gang on boats and attacked the ship. The armed guards on the cargo ship resisted, but the bandits were more numerous and their weapons were confiscated. Then, all the special tax goods on the ship were looted. When troops were dispatched from Wuhan to rescue the ship, the bandits had already fled with their loot. It is reported that several crew members and guards were injured by the bandits.

"Kuailli" Ship Transport: After this incident, Director Li Muqing and the Sichuan cargo owners repeatedly discussed measures to pursue the bandits and deal with the aftermath. In addition to requesting the Wuhan Garrison Command to send troops to suppress the bandits and recover the stolen goods, they decided to meet the demands of the Sichuan cargo owners and dispatch larger ships for future transport. However, it was impossible to rent large ships on the upper Yangtze River for the time being. Therefore, Li Muqing negotiated with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in Shanghai to rent a Yangtze River ship to carry the special goods. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has dispatched the Wuhan director to discuss the arrangements with Li Muqing: (1) In order to ensure tax revenue, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will allocate the "Kuailli" ship to carry the special goods. However, the "Kuailli" ship cannot be fully allocated. Only 5/10 of the ship's capacity will be reserved for special tax goods per trip, and the rest will be used to carry commercial goods. (2) The water freight for the special tax goods from Yichang to Wuhan will be 6.5 taels of silver per dan. (3) The guards stationed on the ship will be appointed by the Special Tax Bureau, and the required food and salaries will be borne by the Special Tax Bureau. It is reported that the above arrangements have been agreed upon by both parties, and the contract will be signed and implemented soon. As for the grounded "Shudu" ship, the Special Tax Bureau will send another tugboat to rescue it.

Letter Requesting the Recall of the Xunyang Anti-Smuggling Squad 185

Finance Minister Song's Letter to General Commander Chiang

Finance Minister Song Ziwen wrote to General Commander Chiang, stating that the original customs anti-smuggling teams under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance have been established since the late Qing Dynasty. All officers and soldiers were either reorganized from the remnants of the military or recruited from drifters with no military training or service knowledge. Their monthly salaries were also extremely meager, so the chiefs in various places regarded encroachment on quotas and private collection of loopholes as normal, and the soldiers relied on covering up private loopholes to supplement their tax revenue. Not only could they not protect the revenue, but they also eroded it. Corruption and decline have reached the extreme. Ziwen is determined to rectify this situation and has instructed the anti-smuggling officers to strictly supervise in order to revitalize the system and achieve results, but to little effect. This is because the habits of the past are deeply ingrained and difficult to change. The annual losses in salt tax are staggering. After exhausting all sources, he knows that nothing short of a fundamental redesign can rectify the situation and protect the source of tax revenue. Since the spring of this year, he has begun to reorganize the special anti-smuggling teams. Everything is done in accordance with military treatment, with the aim of creating an exemplary anti-smuggling force and washing away the evils of the past. Three regiments have been formed. At that time, the war against the rebels was in full swing, and all the troops were transferred to the front. Shanghai and Songhu were quite empty, and the anti-smuggling team had to maintain a part of the security on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line. Subsequently, a part of the old anti-smuggling team in Huaibei rebelled, and the garrison in Haizhou had all been sent to the front line, so the first regiment was transferred to suppress the rebellion in Huaihe. The tax revenue of several million yuan per month was not affected. Moreover, the bandits in Jiangxi province took the opportunity to be rampant, and Jiujiang was in danger. Zhu, the former president, the chief of staff, and Chairman Lu discussed with Ziwen and temporarily transferred the second and third regiments to Jiujiang for defense. Since they were stationed there, they have been deterring and blocking the bandits. There have been no oversights. Now that the military situation has stabilized, the troops on the front line are returning one after another, and the salt tax on various shores urgently needs to be reorganized, and reorganization must start with anti-smuggling. All two regiments stationed in the bay must be dispersed to various salt areas to implement improved anti-smuggling duties. It is proposed to ask your Excellency to quickly dispatch capable troops to Jiujiang to take over defense, so that they can be dispatched and transferred as soon as possible to maintain the source of tax revenue. Respectfully submitted, Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Chiang.

Silk factories in Shanghai have suffered huge losses due to the sharp drop in sales of foreign silk and are unable to maintain operations. The difficulties of the silk industry are indeed a real situation, and landlords and tenants are interdependent, so they express their understanding. The Shanghai Report had previously published a letter from the landlord of Zhenyi Silk Factory in Shanghai agreeing to reduce the factory's rent. "We dare not lag behind and will not be outdone." From this month until May next year, the rent will be reduced.

Central Bank Inspection Report 188

Seventieth Time

The Central Bank's seventieth inspection report on the issuance reserve states that: "In accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this Association is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible bonds of the Bank. The 70th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this Bank on October 31, 1920. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: Total amount of convertible bonds issued: 22,638,292 silver dollars, including 21,694,392 silver dollar bonds and 943,900 copper dollar bonds. Total amount of reserve fund for convertible bonds: 22,638,292 silver dollars, including 20,104,932 silver dollars in cash reserve, of which 15,829,427.27 yuan is stored in the Bank's issuing treasury, 1,014,497 yuan is stored in branches in various ports, and 3,261,007.73 yuan is stored with other banks. The guarantee reserve converted to silver dollars is 2,533,360 yuan. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank's convertible bond regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is inconsistent with the regulations. This report is hereby made. October 31, 1920, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fukun, Supervisors Wang Jingyu, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Zhiqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji."

The third step is from November 20 to November 25. The method is to reprint a number of copies of the cultural institution investigation results revised by each agency for distribution to each district for review. The fourth step is from November 25 to December 10. The method is to order the propaganda committee members of each district and directly affiliated branch to be responsible for re-examining the results of the investigation and to report any additions or deletions in detail as scheduled. The fifth step is from December 10 to the beginning of the third term. The method is for the headquarters to send out forms for investigation or send personnel to inspect and guide at any time.

The Finance, Social Affairs, and Land Bureaus Survey the Disaster in the Pusong District 193

The soil in the 29th and 30th保 of the Pusong District is sandy and barren, and cotton is the main crop. Unexpectedly, the weather during the summer was unusually cold, and after the beginning of autumn, it suddenly became extremely hot again, and most of the cotton plants only flowered but did not bear fruit, or bore fruit that was not substantial. In addition, after the end of summer, a hurricane passed through the area, and continuous rain caused the already formed fruit to rot and fall off. The autumn harvest has become hopeless, with each acre yielding only a few catties or ten catties at most. The farmers in the area are in a disastrous situation and are unable to maintain their livelihoods. The 保, etc., have repeatedly requested the municipal committee member of the area to report the situation to the municipal government and asked to send personnel to investigate. The municipal government ordered the finance, social affairs, and land bureaus to send personnel to Pusong at 9:00 AM yesterday to conduct a survey. The municipal committee member Chen Yafu and staff members Wang Tongfu and Chen Zhen led the way to the disaster area for a detailed survey until 8:00 PM. By the time they returned to Pu, it was raining heavily, and all the committee members were soaked.

Ford Aircraft Invited Guests for Test Flight Yesterday 196

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, Ford and Metong Automobile Companies invited guests from all walks of life to ride on a Ford aircraft. At that time, traffic on Hongqiao Road was bustling. More than 200 guests, half Chinese and half foreign, arrived successively. At the entrance to the airfield, company staff greeted the guests and asked them to sign in. Tickets were then distributed in order of arrival, with nine batches of fourteen tickets each. At 2:10 PM, a special flight took off first, carrying Chen Diaoyuan and people from the business community, among others. After everyone was seated, the plane ascended into the sky and headed straight for Shanghai, circling the city once and landing after about fifteen minutes. It then continued to fly up to the ninth flight. The tenth flight was for the company's staff to ride on themselves. Yesterday, the lingering rain had cleared, and the north wind was howling, with a biting cold that resembled early winter. The aircraft was sturdy in construction, well-equipped, and had several hundred horsepower. Therefore, even when braving the strong winds, it could take flight and remain as stable as a rock, and the passengers experienced no bumpy discomfort. Looking out the window, the city's scenery was clearly visible, with buildings and pavilions, as well as vegetable plots and fields outside the city, scattered like stars. By the end of the test flight, the clock struck five, and guests continued to arrive in droves. It is said that the company may hold a second invitation next week.

Husband Sells Wife into Prostitution 199

Seizes Opportunity to Escape, Barely Recovering Her Senses

Thinks Back and Forth, Bursting into Tears

Ji Zhu, a woman from Nantong, is eighteen years old and extremely beautiful. Her husband, Ji Chun, is addicted to opium. The couple lived in Nanjing. Ji Chun had no permanent property or savings, and he was usually unreliable, so he lacked a proper job. The family situation became increasingly difficult, and borrowing and mortgaging were exhausted. Unable to continue living, he exhausted his mind and devised a plan to lure his wife to Shanghai for fun. After arriving in Shanghai on the 17th of this month, they stayed in a small inn. On the 23rd, he colluded with his friend Zhou Daosan to secretly sell his wife into a certain brothel in the French Concession to be a prostitute, receiving a price of eighty yuan. After obtaining the money, he secretly returned to his hometown. The woman, after entering the brothel, was initially at a loss. When the madam told her the reason, she realized that she had fallen into a fiery pit. However, she could not call for help and could only lament her fate. The madam was extremely violent and would whip her if she slightly disobeyed her when receiving guests. The woman had suffered greatly for several days and could not bear it. She wanted to escape, but the guards were very strict, and there was no plan to escape. Until about 7:00 PM the night before, she took advantage of a slight lapse in the vigilance of the prostitutes and servants and escaped. She rushed to the Datong Pier in the Nanshi area and boarded the Longda steamship, intending to return to her hometown. After boarding the ship, she barely recovered her senses. Thinking back and forth, she couldn't help but feel sad and burst into tears. Yang Yinting, a water patrol officer from the Municipal Security Bureau, heard about it and rushed onto the ship to inquire about her background. The woman cried and sobbed as she told her story. Seeing her situation, Officer Yang felt pity for her and immediately led a team to wait for Chief Xu to conduct a preliminary hearing before finding a way to help her.

Public Concession Vehicle Accident Cases in October 203

13 Deaths and 361 Injuries

According to statistics from the Traffic Department of the Public Concession Police, there were a total of 1,014 vehicle accident cases in the concession in October, with 13 deaths, 361 injuries, and material losses of no less than several thousand yuan. Including the previous nine months, there have been a total of 9,079 accident cases, with 121 deaths and 3,388 injuries. Since the total number of accidents throughout the entire year last year was only 9,691, with 141 deaths and 3,447 injuries, it is expected that the number of accidents, deaths, and injuries this year will exceed last year. A brief analysis of the vehicles involved in the accidents that month shows that automobiles alone accounted for 795 cases, with 242 injuries and 11 deaths. In addition, there were 516 cases involving human-powered vehicles, with 48 injuries; 163 cases involving bicycles, with 46 injuries; 48 cases involving buses, with 19 injuries and 1 death; and 129 cases involving trams, with 31 injuries and 1 death. Nanjing Road, North Sichuan Road, Tibet Road, and Broadway Road are still the most accident-prone areas. In addition, the Bund also had a number of accidents. Pedestrians and vehicles passing through the above roads should be careful and slow down to avoid danger. The French Concession Police Vehicle Department statistics show that there were a total of 101 vehicle accident cases in the concession in October, with 3 deaths and 36 injuries.

Rickshaw Industry Requests Reiteration of the Prohibition of Gang Police Hitting Vehicles 204

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, on the 31st of this month, we received a letter from the Rickshaw Trade Association stating that the association has repeatedly received reports from members that Hua Jie gang police have destroyed vehicles and stained the rickshaw cushions. The rickshaw pullers are unable to resist and have to endure their actions, while the rickshaw owners suffer invisible losses because of their investment. They request relief, etc. Upon arrival at the association, we found that the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau had clearly prohibited gang police from hitting vehicles and destroying property. Rickshaw pullers, driven by their livelihood, often pick up passengers at places where trams and cars stop. Their hasty glances often obstruct traffic, which is both annoying and pitiful. Gang police, due to their duties, should be calm and gentle in directing them to gradually comply while maintaining traffic, without losing sight of the poor people's situation. If they indiscriminately use their batons or hit and stain their rickshaw cushions, causing the general coolie rickshaws to flee in all directions without being spared, it would be inhumane. Moreover, destroying people's property is also prohibited by law. Based on the aforementioned circumstances, it is reasonable to request your bureau to urge the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau to reiterate the previous order and order all districts to pay close attention to it in order to sympathize with the coolies and maintain commercial hardship, which would be a public convenience, etc. Upon arrival at the association, we found that gang police should only gently direct rickshaw pullers to maintain street traffic and vehicle order and should not vent their anger and indiscriminately strike vehicles and stain rickshaw cushions, resulting in the destruction of other people's property and laws, causing rickshaw owners to suffer unwarranted losses. Although your bureau has issued a ban on this matter, gang police are accustomed to doing so, and it is difficult to change their accumulated habits. It is reported that such incidents are still frequently seen. In order to protect rickshaw merchants and rickshaw pullers from extra-legal losses, it seems necessary to reiterate the ban. Accordingly, we hereby inform your bureau of the situation and request that you notify all districts to reissue the previous ban and conduct timely and effective inspections in order to alleviate commercial hardship and promote public friendship."

The Municipal Council Board of Directors has now approved the company to broadcast the string music performed by the Municipal Council Orchestra at the Grand Theatre this season without paying fees or granting exclusive rights.

Continued Request to Strictly Prohibit Garbage from Being Dumped into the Huangpu River 206

Shipping representative Xing Zhigang and others previously stated that the garbage in the urban area of the city has always been piled up on Longhua Mouth. Recently, the boatmen have been lazy and do not rake the garbage up and pile it up again, but instead dump it all into the Huangpu River. Therefore, they submitted a request to the municipal government to find a way to improve the situation, which has been reported in previous newspapers. It is now learned that a part of the area is leased to the French Concession for piling up garbage, and the boatmen are even more unscrupulous, often transporting garbage to the waters near Gaochang Temple and dumping it arbitrarily during high tide, day and night. If this continues, the Huangpu River in that section will inevitably become increasingly shallow, hindering shipping and affecting commerce, which is expected. Yesterday, the representatives submitted another request to the municipal government to request that measures be taken to rectify the situation and strictly prohibit the dumping, as follows: "Respectfully, for the matter of garbage boatmen and servants disobeying the prohibition and still dumping garbage into the Huangpu River, please order the Health and Public Works Bureaus to strictly prohibit it in order to maintain water traffic. We previously contracted with the city and special district to hire boats to transport garbage to Longhua Mouth to unload at the old garbage dump. Later, because no one was in charge, the boatmen were lazy and unwilling to unload and rake it up, so they simply dumped all the garbage into the Huangpu River, causing the Huangpu River to become increasingly shallow and hindering navigation. We submitted a report to your office on October 13 to review and handle the matter. Unexpectedly, we have recently seen garbage boats still heading south during the day's high tide, passing Gaochang Temple and the Jiangnan Shipyard, and then dumping garbage into the Huangpu River one after another. The river is full of floating garbage, drifting with the tide. Many garbage boats do not have boat licenses, so they are blatantly unscrupulous. Considering that the combined population of the city and special district is about 2 million, the amount of garbage discarded every day must be considerable. Why is there no new accumulation of garbage at the designated location of Longhua Mouth? It must have sunk to the bottom of the Huangpu River without a doubt. It is also heard that the garbage boatmen, because it is inconvenient to dump during the daytime low tide, still take advantage of the night tide to dump it. This saying comes from the fishing boat households along the Xiajiazui River, who say that countless garbage enters their nets during the night high tide, and the nets are repeatedly broken. This is ironclad evidence of dumping garbage. Shanghai garbage contains bricks, tiles, gravel, coal, and sand, which are heavy and sink without a trace as soon as they are dumped. As for the light and floating objects such as reeds, white shells, firewood, and grass, they are not easy to sink and often hinder the wheels and rudders of ships. If they are blown by strong winds, they will accumulate and stagnate on the beaches along the river, endangering water conservancy. In view of this situation, we jointly submit another report to your office, respectfully requesting your approval to quickly order the Health Bureau to take measures to rectify the situation and order the Public Works Bureau to number the boats, dispatch boats for inspection, and strictly prohibit the dumping. At the same time, we also consult the French Municipal Council to jointly rectify the situation in order to maintain municipal administration and benefit shipping. We cannot bear to wait for your orders."

Murderer in the Triumph Road Blood Case Sentenced to Life Imprisonment 207

Wang Abing, Zhang Amao, and Gui Jinhua, thieves from Ningbo, robbed the British citizens Roland and Ms. Thomson of their property and shot and killed Thomson and injured Roland on Triumph Road in Shanghai West on the evening of October 3, 1928. After the case, the detectives from the Laozha Police Station investigated and arrested the three criminals, Wang, etc., and sent them to the former Provisional Court for interrogation. They were sentenced to death and reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for review. However, there were still doubts about Wang Abing's part, and the case was returned to the Special District Court for retrial. The trial has now concluded. Yesterday morning, Judge Xu Jiashi of the Criminal Court took his seat and announced the verdict: Wang Abing was sentenced to life imprisonment for jointly robbing and killing Thomson and sentenced to 18 years imprisonment for jointly robbing and attempting to kill Roland. The life imprisonment will be carried out.

All of his money disappeared without a trace. I returned to the hotel and thought about it over and over again. I really felt ashamed to return home and see people, so I took this step, etc. The police chief, seeing his pitiful state, ordered Chinese detective Wu Rongsheng to send him to the Ningbo Fellow Association yesterday morning to find a way to help him.

Old Swindler 210

Women are Most Easily Deceived

Recently, the world is deteriorating, people's hearts are getting worse, and scams are emerging one after another. It is now learned that in recent days, there has been an old man of about sixty years of age in the Chinese and Concession areas of this port, wearing cloth clothes and a black long robe, carrying a cloth bag, with a slight beard, a very simple appearance, and a language that sounds like the Nanhui Chuansha area, etc. He often lingered in the streets and alleys, first scouting and observing at the doors of each household. When he saw that there were only women in the household, he immediately pushed the door in and made a gesture of pity, claiming that he was stranded abroad and lacked funds to return to his hometown, asking for assistance with travel expenses. If there was a screen with an inscription on the guest hall of the household, he would call out the name of the inscription on the screen, saying that Mr. So-and-so also knew him, etc. The women did not know that he was looking at the inscription on the screen and impersonating the name to swindle, and because he was old and honest, they generously gave him two or three yuan in silver. When the head of the household returned home and asked about it, they mostly had no idea and had no such person to know, and they could not figure it out. The day before yesterday, a Chen family in Xiaobeimen, French Concession, was broken into by the old man and swindled out of six jiao of small silver. The next day, a Tong family, who was Chen's neighbor (five households away), was also swindled out of one yuan of silver in the same way. Later, when the two families met and talked about it, they both said it was strange. After studying it again and again, they realized that the name he called out was the inscription on the couplet in the guest hall, so he only swindled women to get his tricks. It is also heard that a Zhou family near Fangbang Bridge also had the same thing happen the day before yesterday. Alas, the treacherousness of people's hearts can be seen here.

Female Worker Swallows Opium, Life in Danger 213

Claimed Her Aunt Asked for Wages But Was Not Given

Took Poison After Being Scolded By Husband

Zhang Tang, a young woman from Ningbo, is 20 years old and lives in a bungalow at No. 106 Tangshan Road, Hongkou. She works as a female worker at the Nanyang Tobacco Company. Her husband, named Defu, is 22 years old and works as a waiter at the Huamao Hotel on the Bund of Renji Road. The day before yesterday (30th) was the end of the month, and the factory paid wages. At 5:30 PM in the evening, she returned home after finishing work. Her aunt immediately asked her for wages. However, because the weather was getting colder, she needed to buy clothes and replied that she had no money this month. There was inevitably a quarrel in the language between aunt and daughter-in-law. When Defu returned home at midnight, her aunt told her son the situation. After listening, Defu scolded his wife slightly. She felt depressed and secretly went out to buy opium in order to die. It was not until 12:00 PM the next day that someone noticed and sent her to Tongren Hospital by car and then to Guangren Hospital for treatment. Because she had been poisoned for too long, her life was in danger.
